
-----title
镇江（丹阳） (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f882ad32a8d44ce1aa07032fce7db532_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f882ad32a8d44ce1aa07032fce7db532");'><span id='f882ad32a8d44ce1aa07032fce7db532_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　本年生。父皋，母李氏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=763')">760-763年</a>　居润州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>　薛十九罢砀山尉过访，有诗赠别。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=766')">765-766年</a>　居润州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a>　父卒于丹徒，李华为撰墓表而殡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=772')">768-772年</a>　居润州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年</a>　少年时，曾流寓丰城龙雾渡。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0d29c9062aac403095d5b0ee09cb8441_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0d29c9062aac403095d5b0ee09cb8441");'><span id='0d29c9062aac403095d5b0ee09cb8441_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=780')">774-780年</a>，16-22岁</div><div id='0d29c9062aac403095d5b0ee09cb8441' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年7月</a>　七月，县丞卢岘卒，为撰墓志铭。作品：润州丹阳县丞卢君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1369772' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369772' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369772?labeling=true' target='_blank'>润州丹阳县丞卢君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（774年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369772")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1369772_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1369772'>君讳岘。字某。范阳人。自魏已降。官婚人物。为天下清甲。大略书于国史。详言在乎家牒。今所书三叶。自曾王父卫州司马府君讳宏寿。初贞晦不仕。公车徵拜。生冀州信都主簿府君讳友裕。友裕生扬州高邮县令府君讳相。君即高邮之第若干子。奉前人之业。讲先师之训。以之克家。以之从政。直方谦厚。卑不可踰。筮仕三次。不离州县之职。曰亳州蒙城县主簿。楚州宝应县尉。润州丹阳县丞。宽敬𦲷事。不希名誉。故每当廉问荐延之日。使臣陟明之举。皆迁延晦避。时议多之。清行懿名。竟用不振。以大历九年七月日。寝疾终于官舍。享年五十五。其嫠陇西李氏。柔顺有妇行。嗣子某等。决于蓍蔡。衔恤襄事。以关河不靖。未克归祔。遂以某月日。权厝于县之北原焉。从宜也。予侨居丹阳。尝与君游。故粗书事实。以备刻石。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1369772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369772'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369772'>生死沄沄，如环斯循。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1369772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1369772'>吁嗟卢君，于此归根。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1369772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1369772'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1369772_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年7月</a>　时已有文名，编所作文字为《童蒙集》十卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　居润州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　居丹阳，作舅母卢氏墓志。作品：润州丹阳县尉李公夫人范阳卢氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1369783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>润州丹阳县尉李公夫人范阳卢氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（776年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369783")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369783_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1369783'>夫人姓卢氏。范阳人。北齐黄门侍郎思道之五代孙也。曾祖悌。皇高道不仕。祖纲。皇城门郎。父侑。皇太原县尉。虽仕皆数命。以至沦谢。而皆饰行懿文。有当时之誉。明德奕世。诞生夫人。既笄。嫔于李公。李公为乌程丹阳二县尉。夫人居贫守约。动必由礼。谦敬以睦中外。吉蠲以奉蒸尝。甘粝粱。服浣濯。中馈式叙。和乐嘻嘻。有嘉闻而无攸遂。一纪于兹矣。尝闻善馀庆。谦受益。岂前志之谬欤。将有必定之数欤。既而奄忽遘疾。不翌日而大渐。以大历十一年月日殁于丹阳之私第。享年若干。以某月日。权厝于县西之五里原。从宜也。生子数人。早岁夭落。今之存者。女子三人。长者生才六霜。其次差以幼矣。虽礼所未及。而号不绝声。呱呱然行路为之憯戚。公以为鼓盆伤神。两不中节。而钟情之哀。可胜既乎。且虞陵谷之变也。乃命权氏甥德舆为之铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1369783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369783'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369783'>去夏屋之渠渠兮。即孤邱之峨峨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369783_comment'></div>往不可复兮。沈痛如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369783_comment'></div>薤露蒿里兮。古有哀歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369783_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1369783_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=779')">777-779年</a>　居润州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年</a>　游刺史马炫之门，与其族子马正字交往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年2月</a>　二月，柳载黜陟江东，表荐试秘书省校书郎，有书申谢。作品：与黜陟使柳谏议书。<div id='poem_1369581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与黜陟使柳谏议书</a><span class='authorDate'>（780年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369581")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369581'>某月日。试秘书省校书郎权德舆上书阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369581_comment'></div>德舆材术无闻。重以拙讷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369581_comment'></div>虽星轺往复。皆获趋拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369581_comment'></div>竟未得粗承馀论。少尽下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369581_comment'></div>伏蒙以通世之旧。将献状受禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369581_comment'></div>感戴循环。不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369581_comment'></div>或有所见。敢布愚衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369581_comment'></div>何者。今皇帝驭天下之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369581_comment'></div>将欲拔才俊。延幽滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369581_comment'></div>综覈名实。览观风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369581_comment'></div>故分诏近臣。省问四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369581_comment'></div>将天之命。其旨不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369581_comment'></div>则阁下举一士。用一贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369581_comment'></div>必当穷验声实。精究终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369581_comment'></div>一旦以愚当荐士之目。诚众多所未喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369581_comment'></div>凡以故旧之私。不能忘情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369581_comment'></div>与夫推贤类能。其事则异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369581_comment'></div>今者澄清省察。以得人为功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369581_comment'></div>直道公议。天下属目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369581_comment'></div>此时而失。则所失多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369581_comment'></div>德舆伏膺儒行。三十未立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369581_comment'></div>拊躬责已。知不如人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369581_comment'></div>俟他时进修。与诸生齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369581_comment'></div>方冀当大君子眷念之至。申鄙夫报效之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369581_comment'></div>今若以赀用所迫。苟进一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369581_comment'></div>则佣书贩舂。亦足自给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369581_comment'></div>必不敢以区区之身。上累名器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369581_comment'></div>敢拒黔敖之食。徐受山涛之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369581_comment'></div>下情所守。在此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369581_comment'></div>是以竟未获拜谢者。以必所不敢当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369581_comment'></div>伏惟宴閒之馀。俯察愚朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369581_comment'></div>文章鄙略。不足以烦省览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369581_comment'></div>用此陈露。惭畏伏深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369581_comment'></div>不宣。德舆再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369581_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1369581_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2beadf4c09594b338d6feee7feba88ac_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2beadf4c09594b338d6feee7feba88ac");'><span id='2beadf4c09594b338d6feee7feba88ac_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=782&endYear=784')">782-784年</a>，24-26岁</div><div id='2beadf4c09594b338d6feee7feba88ac' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=782&endYear=782')">782年</a>　返丹阳，得崔造书议婚，复书承命。作品：答左司崔员外书。<div id='poem_1369584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369584?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答左司崔员外书</a><span class='authorDate'>（782年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369584")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369584'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369584'>德舆器用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1369584", 1369584, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>琐薄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369584_comment'></div>无他才术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369584_comment'></div>徒以木讷之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369584_comment'></div>玩习圣贤之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369584_comment'></div>尝以为大朴久散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369584_comment'></div>世道交丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369584_comment'></div>师友之义缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369584_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1369584", 1369584, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>醨薄</span>之风起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369584_comment'></div>蚩蚩万情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369584_comment'></div>无所思向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369584_comment'></div>衔愤结怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369584_comment'></div>惄然终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369584_comment'></div>前年得以行役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369584_comment'></div>获觏德容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369584_comment'></div>始蒙泛爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369584_comment'></div>竟接清议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369584_comment'></div>初论当世之理要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369584_comment'></div>次陈情性之大端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369584_comment'></div>终语道德之原极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369584_comment'></div>澡雪百虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369584_comment'></div>泊然葆真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369584_comment'></div>一闻至论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369584_comment'></div>神开意警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369584_comment'></div>不觉虚白澄旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369584_comment'></div>浃洽四支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369584_comment'></div>则易直子谅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369584_comment'></div>又其细也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369584_comment'></div>当此之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369584_comment'></div>诚欲备门弟子之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369584_comment'></div>日展严师之敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369584_comment'></div>虽此志不遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369584_comment'></div>实念逾涯忘年之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369584_comment'></div>契比伯仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369584_comment'></div>昨者奉问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369584_comment'></div>洞见仁衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369584_comment'></div>且有退身邱樊之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369584_comment'></div>嚱夫中人之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369584_comment'></div>或不以利回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369584_comment'></div>而多以名败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369584_comment'></div>或时能蹈义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369584_comment'></div>而鲜能克仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369584_comment'></div>此诚细者可力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369584_comment'></div>大端则循情而动矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369584_comment'></div>至于黜聪晦明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369584_comment'></div>恬于退让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369584_comment'></div>息浩然之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369584_comment'></div>哀乐不入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369584_comment'></div>不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369584_comment'></div>则乘时致位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369584_comment'></div>以天下为已任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369584_comment'></div>化醨为醇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369584_comment'></div>泽流无垠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369584_comment'></div>彝伦式叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369584_comment'></div>生生茂遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369584_comment'></div>此诚大君子之出处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369584_comment'></div>近古以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369584_comment'></div>作者实鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369584_comment'></div>岂世运有在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369584_comment'></div>或时无其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369584_comment'></div>间睹皇极综论之一篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369584_comment'></div>得之尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369584_comment'></div>然则或进或退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369584_comment'></div>小屈小伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369584_comment'></div>岂足为执事者道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369584_comment'></div>又示问之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369584_comment'></div>情旨备至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369584_comment'></div>不弃弱植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369584_comment'></div>伸以嘉姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369584_comment'></div>荀陈之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369584_comment'></div>非所敢当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369584_comment'></div>况司徒令子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369584_comment'></div>为后来名辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369584_comment'></div>精识洞鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369584_comment'></div>诚已得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369584_comment'></div>鄙人何堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369584_comment'></div>复当此命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369584_comment'></div>门闾之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1369584_comment'></div>珉玉不侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1369584_comment'></div>将何以祗承厚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369584_comment'></div>当叔宝逸少之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369584_comment'></div>恐累清德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1369584_comment'></div>无任下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1369584_comment'></div>已具咨闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1369584_comment'></div>敬承嘉命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369584_comment'></div>寻冀拜谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369584_comment'></div>感庆伏深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1369584_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_86_1369584_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=783')">783年</a>　在江淮水陆运使幕中。七月，叔父自洛阳往新定，经丹阳，侍宴饯送。作品：秋夜侍姑叔宴会序。<div id='poem_1369611' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369611' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369611?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋夜侍姑叔宴会序</a><span class='authorDate'>（783年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369611")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369611_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369611'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369611'>叔父至自东周。第如新定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369611_comment'></div>就长子桐庐尉之养也。途出云阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369611_comment'></div>德舆之侨居在焉。拜庆之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369611_comment'></div>式展宴饯。掇蔬焚枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369611_comment'></div>以实圆方。叔父诸姑既就坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369611_comment'></div>群从伯仲。或冠或丱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369611_comment'></div>中外稚孺。凡四五十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369611_comment'></div>差其长幼。为侍坐之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369611_comment'></div>畅之以旨酒。既醉不諠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369611_comment'></div>侑之以清弦。中奏弥静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369611_comment'></div>天天申申。其乐无垠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369611_comment'></div>发之于恬旷。得之于名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369611_comment'></div>稍间。则圆魄照坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369611_comment'></div>微风入林。残暑尽销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369611_comment'></div>清光交映。歌诗类事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369611_comment'></div>举节应觞。觉听视之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369611_comment'></div>无非和乐。虽谢庭羯末之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369611_comment'></div>雪花柳絮之兴。及夫情适于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369611_comment'></div>率礼无违。亦一时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369611_comment'></div>乃命编次其文。且书其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369611_comment'></div>时建中四年之七月。德舆操觚以序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369611_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1369611_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=783')">783年</a>　在丹阳送许孟容赴李皋江西节度使幕。作品：送许校书赴江西使府序；月夜泛舟重送许校书联句序。<div id='poem_1369629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369629' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369629")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369629_comment'></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1369629_comment'></div>必以射策东堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369629_comment'></div>校文石渠为称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369629_comment'></div>于公范言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369629_comment'></div>皆其细者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369629_comment'></div>予与公范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369629_comment'></div>寻世好以约交道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369629_comment'></div>获申十年之敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369629_comment'></div>出处多故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369629_comment'></div>及兹再会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369629_comment'></div>久饱诸公之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369629_comment'></div>今日得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369629_comment'></div>心包大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369629_comment'></div>口析精理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369629_comment'></div>可以稽合同异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369629_comment'></div>悬照是非。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369629_comment'></div>疾若机响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369629_comment'></div>不亦宜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369629_comment'></div>国家尚用兵车之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369629_comment'></div>且思磐石之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369629_comment'></div>俾贤王秉旄节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369629_comment'></div>主江西诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369629_comment'></div>辟书四下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369629_comment'></div>大搜隽望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369629_comment'></div>公范拂拭缝掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369629_comment'></div>从容长裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369629_comment'></div>赴知己之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369629_comment'></div>伸丈夫之志。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369629_comment'></div>礼让兴行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369629_comment'></div>且以中庸明诚之根本。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369629_comment'></div>固在于远者大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369629_comment'></div>庸讵知今兹一举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369629_comment'></div>非图南之羊角耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369629_comment'></div>临歧话别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369629_comment'></div>迭以勉固志业而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369629_comment'></div>若愀然涕下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369629_comment'></div>以聚散为念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369629_comment'></div>此可略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369629_comment'></div>众君子置之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1369629_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1369630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>月夜泛舟重送许校书联句序</a><span "poem_title_1369630")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369630'>公范持江西辟书。驾言即路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369630_comment'></div>其出处之迹。与婉婉之画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369630_comment'></div>鄙人不腆。已为之序引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369630_comment'></div>且吴抵钟陵。二千里而遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369630_comment'></div>凡我诸生。怆离宴之不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369630_comment'></div>故再徵斯会。秋月若昼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369630_comment'></div>方舟溯沿。笑言不哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369630_comment'></div>引满造适。公范乃握管作三字丽句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369630_comment'></div>仆与二三子联而继之。申之以四五六七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369630_comment'></div>以广其事。如其风烟月露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369630_comment'></div>与行者居者之思。各见于词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369630_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1369630_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=783')">783年</a>　十月，包佶财赋为陈少游劫夺，辗转往江西。遂出幕，居丹阳。去职时朝衔仍为右金吾卫兵曹参军。作品：自杨子归丹阳初遂闲居聊呈惠公。<div id='poem_19386' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=784&endYear=784')">784年3月</a>　三月，杜佑任广州刺史、岭南节度使，辟为从事，以疾辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=784&endYear=784')">784年</a>　在丹阳送从姨弟王仲舒往衢州。作品：送王仲舒侍从赴衢州觐叔父序。<div id='poem_1369656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王仲舒侍从赴衢州觐叔父序</a><span class='authorDate'>（784年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369656")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369656'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369656'>士有抗方外之迹。以世教为桎梏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369656_comment'></div>不然。则必由于文章之途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369656_comment'></div>以其合大中之道。天理发于心术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369656_comment'></div>周于事业。此贤士君子之所以致思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369656_comment'></div>太原王生仲舒。从事于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369656_comment'></div>弱冠秀发。始以雅词一轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369656_comment'></div>为士相见之贽。予尝学于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369656_comment'></div>閒世多病。方将自全于朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369656_comment'></div>止所不知。及览子之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369656_comment'></div>文达而理举。温润博雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369656_comment'></div>且多古风。则曩时之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369656_comment'></div>斐然复生。所守不固然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369656_comment'></div>然则文变损益。非鄙所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369656_comment'></div>粗言士友出处之略。用以为赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369656_comment'></div>动而不皦。静而不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369656_comment'></div>而不峻。通而不杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369656_comment'></div>此吾徒之所夙夜也。固在子之彀中耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369656_comment'></div>行旅之虞。不足以诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369656_comment'></div>执事自由拳抵信安。途不千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369656_comment'></div>奉板舆之欢。赴竹林之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369656_comment'></div>况新安江路。水石清浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369656_comment'></div>严陵故台。德风蔼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369656_comment'></div>渔浦潭七里濑。皆此路也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369656_comment'></div>二谢清兴。多自兹始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369656_comment'></div>今日出祖。可以言诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369656_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1369656_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a0d78889023d45e99b9dd40e8f62e8f3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a0d78889023d45e99b9dd40e8f62e8f3");'><span id='a0d78889023d45e99b9dd40e8f62e8f3_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=785')">785年</a>　闲居丹阳，与李畅游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=785')">785年</a>　冬，独孤氏女生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=786&endYear=786')">786年2月</a>　二月，外舅崔造拜相，有书致贺。作品：贺崔相国书。<div id='poem_1369588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺崔相国书</a><span class='authorDate'>（786年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369588")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369588'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369588'>伏惟大方全德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369588_comment'></div>自中发外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369588_comment'></div>蕴为志气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369588_comment'></div>播为事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369588_comment'></div>然则阜庶生物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369588_comment'></div>操持化权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369588_comment'></div>结于众心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369588_comment'></div>为日固久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369588_comment'></div>且大贤之出处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369588_comment'></div>天下之否泰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369588_comment'></div>故诏下之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369588_comment'></div>人人相庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369588_comment'></div>又早岁获睹皇极综论元德志孤云赋凄风诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369588_comment'></div>伏读累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369588_comment'></div>备见精虑之所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369588_comment'></div>言理乱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369588_comment'></div>多推世运于必然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369588_comment'></div>殊不知弛张变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369588_comment'></div>存乎其人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369588_comment'></div>自古哲贤之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369588_comment'></div>或尚志不展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369588_comment'></div>郁堙当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369588_comment'></div>长叹痛哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369588_comment'></div>于是乎作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369588_comment'></div>伏惟以常所感慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369588_comment'></div>申于盛明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369588_comment'></div>使三辰光润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369588_comment'></div>万方轨道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369588_comment'></div>实在指顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369588_comment'></div>岂逃彀中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369588_comment'></div>且以西汉公辅言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369588_comment'></div>萧曹以清静熙帝载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369588_comment'></div>良平以谟明赞王业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369588_comment'></div>至宣帝时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369588_comment'></div>则魏相通故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369588_comment'></div>邴吉知大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369588_comment'></div>斯皆章章可言者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369588_comment'></div>洎夫张苍之律历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369588_comment'></div>孙宏之文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369588_comment'></div>韦贤之好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369588_comment'></div>平当之有耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369588_comment'></div>然亦号为贤相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369588_comment'></div>抑又次焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369588_comment'></div>至若匡张孔马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369588_comment'></div>服儒衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369588_comment'></div>被阿谀之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369588_comment'></div>不胜其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369588_comment'></div>最下则陶青刘舍庄翟赵周之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369588_comment'></div>皆龌龊备位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369588_comment'></div>故身名偕泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369588_comment'></div>夫此数子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369588_comment'></div>岂不粗知君臣之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369588_comment'></div>古今之变哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369588_comment'></div>病于无所发明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369588_comment'></div>保持禄位而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369588_comment'></div>有时无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369588_comment'></div>可不谓大哀乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369588_comment'></div>又古人有立德立功立言之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369588_comment'></div>顾惟多幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369588_comment'></div>获览炳然之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369588_comment'></div>又备陈馀论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369588_comment'></div>有以见大君子遣辞发虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369588_comment'></div>宏裕溥博者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369588_comment'></div>惟德与功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369588_comment'></div>实在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369588_comment'></div>洒天下耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369588_comment'></div>复万物于全性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369588_comment'></div>在丈人践而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369588_comment'></div>守而终之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369588_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369588_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_70_1369588_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=786&endYear=786')">786年</a>　秋，李畅招游马迹山，以病不克偕往。旋得江西观察使李兼辟书。作品：酬李二十二兄主簿马迹山见寄。<div id='poem_19645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_19645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/19645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬李二十二兄主簿马迹山见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（786年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_19645")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_19645_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_19645'>族内兄畅，纯静而深，直方而文，与予同偶居丹阳。丹阳郭北四十里所，有马迹山。山有奇峰怪石，且多昔贤真仙之所游践。方外士殷涣然，通《易经》、老、严之旨，居于山下。从舅原均，探异好古，亦往来栖息其间。贞元元年，兄以典校秘书，调补江陵松滋主簿，以地远不就职。予以环卫冗秩，罢漕挽从事，且久家居食贫，里巷相接。其明年，兄命驾游此山，予以疾故，不克偕往。既而猥辱钟陵檄召，兄自山中以诗一首见贻。理精词达，清涤心府。三复其文，如至山下。终篇则戏以出处之迹见诮。故予复之于此章，仍加六十字以就全数。</div><div id='poem_preface_19645_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_19645'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3361, "poem_allusion_19645")'>谷口</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_19645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_19645'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_19645'>杳杳尘外想，悠悠区中缘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_19645'>如何战未胜，曾是教所牵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_19645'>远郊有灵峰，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_19645", 19645, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>夙昔</span>栖真仙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_19645'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_19645", 19645, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>鸾声</span>去已久，马迹空依然。<div id='poem_sentence_3_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_19645'>丹崖转初旭，碧落凝秋烟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_19645'>松风共箫飒，萝月想婵娟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_19645'>内兄蕴遐心，嘉遁性所便。<div id='poem_sentence_6_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_19645'>不能栖枳棘，且复探云泉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_19645'>中有冥寂人，闲读逍遥篇。<div id='poem_sentence_8_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_19645'>联袂共支策，抠衣赏绝编。<div id='poem_sentence_9_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_19645'>徐行石上苔，静韵风中弦。<div id='poem_sentence_10_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_19645'>烟霞湿儒服，日月生寥天。<div id='poem_sentence_11_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_19645'>新诗来起予，璀璨六义全。<div id='poem_sentence_12_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_19645'>能尽含写意，转令山水鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_13_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_19645'>若闻笙鹤声，宛在耳目前。<div id='poem_sentence_14_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_19645'>登攀阻心赏，愁绝空怀贤。<div id='poem_sentence_15_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_19645'>出处岂异途，心冥即真筌。<div id='poem_sentence_16_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_19645'>暂从西府檄，终卧东菑田。<div id='poem_sentence_17_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_19645'>不嫌予步蹇，但恐君行膻。<div id='poem_sentence_18_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_19645'>如能固旷怀，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3361, "poem_sentence_19_19645")'>谷口</span>期穷年。<div id='poem_sentence_19_19645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_19645'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_19645_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='829e9e40e6eb4a1aa2e29120a1c0a291_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("829e9e40e6eb4a1aa2e29120a1c0a291");'><span id='829e9e40e6eb4a1aa2e29120a1c0a291_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=788&endYear=790')">788-790年</a>，30-32岁</div><div id='829e9e40e6eb4a1aa2e29120a1c0a291' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=788&endYear=788')">788年6月</a>　六月，太夫人病故，奉丧返葬丹阳，遂居丹阳丁忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=789&endYear=789')">789年</a>　春，葬太夫人于丹阳，请梁肃作墓志。居丹阳丁忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=790&endYear=790')">790年</a>　正月，为友人戴叔伦撰墓志铭。时居丹阳丁母忧。作品：朝散大夫使持节都督容州诸军事守容州刺史兼侍御史充本管经略招讨制置等使谯县开国男赐紫金鱼袋戴公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1369761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369761?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散大夫使持节都督容州诸军事守容州刺史兼侍御史充本管经略招讨制置等使谯县开国男赐紫金鱼袋戴公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（790年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369761")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1369761_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1369761'>维贞元五年夏四月。容州刺史经略使侍御史谯县男戴公至部之三月。以疾受代。回车瓯骆。六月甲申。次于清远峡而薨。春秋五十八。明年正月庚申。返葬于金坛玉京原之旧封。宜叙世德。以识幽穸云。公讳叔伦。字幼公。本谯国人。其先在宋为公族。于汉为儒宗。东汉则有司徒涉。西晋则有司农𨔵。𨔵后南渡。始居丹徒。八叶至宋临湘侯明宝。明宝曾孙梁左丞皓。皓元孙皇德州司士好问。公之曾王父也。王父修誉。父慎用。皆自縻天爵。不顾翘车。传次君之礼文。尽通奥旨。师安道之晦德。尤恶知名。故世风纯庆。及公而发。公早以词艺振嘉闻。中以材术商功利。终以理行敷教化。师履素王之训。周旋君子之儒。淑声休问。苾芬四畅。初抠衣于兰陵萧茂挺。以文学政事。见称萧门。文本菁华。而长于比兴。粲为采章。锵如珩璜。鼓钟于宫。累辟大府。分命于计相也。则为湖南河内留后。自秘书正字三迁至监察御史。曳裾于贤王也。则为湖南江西上介。由大理寺司直再转至尚书祠部郎中。其阜人成化也。则东阳一同之人沐旬岁之治。抚人饫三年之惠。容人被踰月之教。夔人闻诏而欢。承讣而哀。不及蒙其泽。历官十一。而云安不书。所至之邦。必刻金石。始在转运府也。董赋于南荆。会蜀将杨琳。拥徒阻命。诏书告谕。初无革志。宵引锐卒。劫胁使臣曰。归我金币。可以纾死。公山立不挠。勇生于仁。端其词气。强于师旅。暴叛知感。乞盟于公。黎明。率其徒西向拜泣。指期诣阙。冢臣列状。天子召对。而推功于府。不伐其劳。时谈翕然。勇让具举。其在临川也。清明仁恕。多省费方略。蜀郡崇儒之化。南阳均水之法。精力区处。民以便安。田壤耕辟。狱犴清净。居一年。玺书褒异。就加金紫。未几而有容州之拜。且都督府所治。列城十三。训戎抚俗之任。招徕式遏之寄。非通方明略。无以威怀。盖皇慈所轸。先于柔远。方将布恺悌于夷落。致风俗于休嘉。议者以九伯二男。可跂而至。天则不吊。末如之何。君直清笃厚。博物通理。有大学之明诚。大雅之疏达。静如渊泉。动如镆干。不缁不磷。与令闻终始。起布衣儒服。位视方隅。归全之日。才具祭器。去国见麾幢之盛。返葬备裧輤之仪。列松槚于旧封。展牲牢于新荐。哀荣之礼。乡党称焉。初公娶京兆韦氏。永州刺史采之女。继室以博陵崔氏。殿中侍御史殷之女。皆淑明柔嘉。不幸早世。允子曰郅曰邡。年甫及龀。哀如成人。公仲兄新城长伯伦。以予夙承公欢。且有遗托。既不获让。是用直书。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1369761_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369761'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369761'>信都九江，文礼章章。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1369761'>百代弥光，司徒佐汉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1369761'>司农匡晋，乃炽而昌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1369761'>世无违德，时有通塞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1369761'>或行或藏，克生容州。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1369761'>贵为诸侯，其道直方。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1369761'>政成中和，播为颂歌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1369761'>化被二邦，列爵疏土。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1369761'>灿烂龟组，鸾声锵锵。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1369761'>宜享繁祉，以媚天子。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1369761'>今也则亡，还葬故里。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1369761'>仙山之趾，德音不忘。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1369761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1369761'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1369761_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9e2fdb3342094b479fe29a9527f29b6b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9e2fdb3342094b479fe29a9527f29b6b");'><span id='9e2fdb3342094b479fe29a9527f29b6b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=791&endYear=791')">791年</a>，33岁</div><div id='9e2fdb3342094b479fe29a9527f29b6b' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>返丹阳居。晤诗人秦系于丹徒，为作《秦征君校书与刘随州唱和诗序》<div id='poem_1369598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦徵君校书与刘随州唱和诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（791年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369598")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369598'>儒有秦公绪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369598_comment'></div>当天宝理平之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369598_comment'></div>兴丽则鼓盛名于当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369598_comment'></div>遭多故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369598_comment'></div>道进身退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369598_comment'></div>越部山水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369598_comment'></div>佐其清机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369598_comment'></div>圆冠野服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369598_comment'></div>翛然自放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369598_comment'></div>宅遐心于事外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369598_comment'></div>得佳句于物表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369598_comment'></div>不知华缨丹毂之为贵者几四十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369598_comment'></div>方帅时贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369598_comment'></div>轼闾悬榻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369598_comment'></div>昔郑公通德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369598_comment'></div>有乡门之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369598_comment'></div>秦君丽句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369598_comment'></div>创里亭之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369598_comment'></div>慕风骚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369598_comment'></div>多所向仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369598_comment'></div>贞元中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369598_comment'></div>天下无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369598_comment'></div>大君好文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369598_comment'></div>公绪旧游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369598_comment'></div>多在显列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369598_comment'></div>伯喈文举之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369598_comment'></div>争为荐首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369598_comment'></div>而寿阳大夫公之章先闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369598_comment'></div>故有书府典校之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369598_comment'></div>时动静不滞于一方矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369598_comment'></div>七年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369598_comment'></div>始与予遇于南徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369598_comment'></div>白头初命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369598_comment'></div>色无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1369598", 1369598, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>愠怍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369598_comment'></div>知名岁久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369598_comment'></div>故其相得甚欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369598_comment'></div>因谓予曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369598_comment'></div>今业六义以著称者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369598_comment'></div>必当唱酬往复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369598_comment'></div>亦所以极其思虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369598_comment'></div>较其胜败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369598_comment'></div>而文以时之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369598_comment'></div>闻人序而申之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369598_comment'></div>悉索笈中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369598_comment'></div>得数十编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369598_comment'></div>皆文场之重名强敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369598_comment'></div>且见校以故敌故<span class='inlineComment2'>（二字疑衍）</span>随州刘君长卿赠答之卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369598_comment'></div>惜其长往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369598_comment'></div>谓余宜叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369598_comment'></div>嚱夫彼汉东守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369598_comment'></div>尝自以为五言长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369598_comment'></div>而公绪用偏伍奇师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369598_comment'></div>攻坚击众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369598_comment'></div>虽老益壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369598_comment'></div>未尝顿锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369598_comment'></div>词或约而旨深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369598_comment'></div>类乍近而致远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369598_comment'></div>若珩佩之清越相激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369598_comment'></div>类组绣之元黄相发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369598_comment'></div>奇采逸响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369598_comment'></div>争为前驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369598_comment'></div>至于室家离合之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369598_comment'></div>朋友切磋之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369598_comment'></div>咏言其伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369598_comment'></div>折之以正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369598_comment'></div>凡若干首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369598_comment'></div>各见于词云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_66_1369598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>诏以太常博士征入朝，携眷赴京。至西岳庙停车祝谒。<br /></div>
-----end

扬州

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年</a>　在扬州杜佑幕中，署朝职为试右金吾卫兵曹参军。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='433cd37c76644425bb4b96c44557c334_label'><a href='javascript: gray;'>▪</span>正月，李兼征为国子祭酒，府罢。时任观察支使，带宪职为监察御史里行。裴胄继任江西观察使，与淮南节度使杜佑辟书同日至京，遂应杜佑辟。作品：从事淮南府过亡友杨校书旧厅感念愀然遂书十韵。<div id='poem_19529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_19529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/19529?labeling=true' target='_blank'>从事淮南府过亡友杨校书旧厅感念愀然<span class='inlineComment2'>（一下有遂书十韵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（791年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_content_19529'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_19529'>故人随化往，倏忽今六霜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_19529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_19529'>及我就拘限，清风留此堂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_19529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_19529'>松竹逾映蔚<span id='poem_sentence_5_19529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_19529'>正平赋鹦鹉，文考<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8055, id='poem_sentence_8_19529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_19529'>岂必限宿草，含悽<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作泪）</span>洒衣裳。<div 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，与同僚薛七沿江泛舟下，旋闻李兼丧。<br /></div>

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='83f943fc3427436e84d3603d61dfd24e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("83f943fc3427436e84d3603d61dfd24e");'><span id='83f943fc3427436e84d3603d61dfd24e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年</a>，23岁</div><div id='83f943fc3427436e84d3603d61dfd24e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年9月</a>　秋，行役江西南昌，渡江南下。九月，道经杭州，值刺史元全柔调任黔中经略使，预祖饯，作序送行。复经睦州。作品：奉送黔中元中丞赴本道序。<div id='poem_1369605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉送黔中元中丞赴本道序</a><span class='authorDate'>（781年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369605")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369605'>中丞顷持邦宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369605_comment'></div>灵台坦荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369605_comment'></div>中立不倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369605_comment'></div>公辅之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369605_comment'></div>悬于人心者久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369605_comment'></div>大方夷道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369605_comment'></div>且无町畦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369605_comment'></div>持刀笔者忮害为狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369605_comment'></div>故前言有馀杭之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369605_comment'></div>左迁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369605_comment'></div>大君端拱穆清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369605_comment'></div>深恤人隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369605_comment'></div>虑远黎之未康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369605_comment'></div>择可以富教之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369605_comment'></div>以馀杭风政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369605_comment'></div>表课第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369605_comment'></div>故有持节黔中之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369605_comment'></div>天之爱人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369605_comment'></div>斯谓甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369605_comment'></div>受命之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369605_comment'></div>庀徒戒行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369605_comment'></div>鄙人以使者之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369605_comment'></div>假道于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369605_comment'></div>属当祖軷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369605_comment'></div>辱在宾筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369605_comment'></div>敢宣言于执事曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369605_comment'></div>夫蹈全德者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369605_comment'></div>事无夷险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369605_comment'></div>播善政者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369605_comment'></div>地无遐迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369605_comment'></div>然则五溪之氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369605_comment'></div>其将泰乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369605_comment'></div>吕梁悬水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369605_comment'></div>尚在忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369605_comment'></div>矧夫巴黔故地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369605_comment'></div>方镇专达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369605_comment'></div>惠饫夷落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369605_comment'></div>兴行礼让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369605_comment'></div>然后翱翔清朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369605_comment'></div>羽仪百僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369605_comment'></div>倚伏之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369605_comment'></div>庸讵知不以此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369605_comment'></div>夫临觞捧袂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369605_comment'></div>愀然悽怆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369605_comment'></div>此儿女之仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369605_comment'></div>固壮夫耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369605_comment'></div>愚亦耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369605_comment'></div>引满举白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369605_comment'></div>既醉而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369605_comment'></div>文则不腆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369605_comment'></div>盖指事云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1369605_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
建德（睦州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='afd24311a99744ee93ab44cff6d90d9e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("afd24311a99744ee93ab44cff6d90d9e");'><span id='afd24311a99744ee93ab44cff6d90d9e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年</a>，23岁</div><div id='afd24311a99744ee93ab44cff6d90d9e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年</a>　秋，行役江西南昌，渡江南下。九月，道经杭州，值刺史元全柔调任黔中经略使，预祖饯，作序送行。复经睦州。<br /></div>

-----title
鄱阳（饶州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='95dc1cc821644d05b4cc84835a06202f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("95dc1cc821644d05b4cc84835a06202f");'><span id='95dc1cc821644d05b4cc84835a06202f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年</a>，23岁</div><div id='95dc1cc821644d05b4cc84835a06202f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年</a>　经饶州，谒崔造，深见赏爱，约为兄弟，以年辈不伦辞。作品：志过。<div id='poem_1369701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>志过</a><span class='authorDate'>（781年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369701")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369701'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369701'>辛酉岁。予以吏役道于上饶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369701_comment'></div>时左司郎中博陵崔公出守郡佐。与予语及世道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369701_comment'></div>次及人伦大节。因曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369701_comment'></div>延州之让。不其至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369701_comment'></div>或者言吴以太伯让而兴。季子让而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369701_comment'></div>此乃徇于一方而不超乎大方也。原夫太伯避季历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369701_comment'></div>奔荆蛮。以就文武之大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369701_comment'></div>则知太伯因天下之尊周以成周也。岂以兴周为念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369701_comment'></div>季子因天下之去让以全让也。岂以亡吴为念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369701_comment'></div>然则太伯季子。皆以天下之心为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369701_comment'></div>兴亡曾不屑虑。彼或者之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369701_comment'></div>诚未通其旨焉。予曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369701_comment'></div>诚哉是言。然季子之历聘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369701_comment'></div>闻乐章。辩歌诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369701_comment'></div>皆审其盛衰。以造乎微精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369701_comment'></div>明闳达物。无所逃数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369701_comment'></div>有所极耳。又何区区异论于其閒哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369701_comment'></div>荅曰。子之言过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369701_comment'></div>若季子以兴亡必然。力不能支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369701_comment'></div>乘此而后三让。是利于将亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369701_comment'></div>因以沽名者也。岂可为君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369701_comment'></div>言之过矣。且以吴之存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369701_comment'></div>而季子亡之。以让之废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369701_comment'></div>而季子全之。向使勤一国之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369701_comment'></div>理于勾吴。今亦化为古墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369701_comment'></div>鞠为榛芜。曷与夫礼让之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369701_comment'></div>使千古是式。贪以之廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369701_comment'></div>暴以之仁。忍垢冒荣者以之知惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369701_comment'></div>其于为理也。不其达欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369701_comment'></div>予乃拜受其论。退书所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369701_comment'></div>且以志过名篇。庶乎闻义能徙之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369701_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1369701_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南昌（豫章）

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=787&endYear=787')">787年1月</a>　正月，戴叔伦坐谤被推案，会得澄清，和陆羽诗同为之庆。作品：同陆太祝鸿渐崔法曹载华见萧侍御留后说得卫抚州报推事使张侍御却回前刺史戴员外无事喜而有作三首；萧侍御喜陆太祝自信州移居洪州玉芝观诗序。<div id='poem_19300' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369599'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369599'>太祝陆君鸿渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369599_comment'></div>以词艺卓异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369599_comment'></div>为当时闻人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369599_comment'></div>凡所至之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369599_comment'></div>必千骑效劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369599_comment'></div>五浆先馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369599_comment'></div>尝考一亩之宫于上饶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369599_comment'></div>时江西上介殿中萧侍御公瑜权领是邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369599_comment'></div>相得欢甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369599_comment'></div>会连帅大司宪李公入觐于王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369599_comment'></div>萧君领廉察留府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369599_comment'></div>太祝亦不远而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369599_comment'></div>声同而应随故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369599_comment'></div>先是尝舍于道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369599_comment'></div>因复居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369599_comment'></div>竹斋虚白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369599_comment'></div>湖水在下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369599_comment'></div>春物萌动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369599_comment'></div>时鸟变声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369599_comment'></div>支颐散发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369599_comment'></div>心目相适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369599_comment'></div>萧君悦其所以然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369599_comment'></div>既展宾主之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369599_comment'></div>又歌诗以将之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369599_comment'></div>其词清越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369599_comment'></div>铿若金璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369599_comment'></div>得诗人之辩丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369599_comment'></div>见君子之交好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369599_comment'></div>诗既成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369599_comment'></div>而太祝有酬和之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369599_comment'></div>复往之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369599_comment'></div>粲然可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369599_comment'></div>客有前法曹掾崔君茂实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369599_comment'></div>文场之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369599_comment'></div>以六义为已任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369599_comment'></div>攘臂拔笔而为和者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369599_comment'></div>惟三贤师友风骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369599_comment'></div>迭为强敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369599_comment'></div>志之所之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369599_comment'></div>发为英声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369599_comment'></div>其于奇正相生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369599_comment'></div>质文相发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369599_comment'></div>若笙磬合奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369599_comment'></div>组缋交映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369599_comment'></div>君子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369599_comment'></div>侍御唱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369599_comment'></div>太祝酬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369599_comment'></div>法曹和之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369599_comment'></div>是三篇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369599_comment'></div>不可以不纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369599_comment'></div>况合散出处之未始有极耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369599_comment'></div>以鄙人尝学于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369599_comment'></div>俾冠以序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369599_comment'></div>其或继而和者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369599_comment'></div>用先成为次序云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1369599_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=787&endYear=787')">787年8月</a>　六月大旱，李兼祈雨于洪州西山风雨池。八月，为之记。作品：洪州西山风雨池记。<div id='poem_1369683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州西山风雨池记</a><span class='authorDate'>（787年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a
