class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369683'>山林川谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369683_comment'></div>能出云为风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369683_comment'></div>皆曰神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369683_comment'></div>诸侯在其地则祭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369683_comment'></div>钟陵风雨池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369683_comment'></div>在西山洪井之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369683_comment'></div>发源山椒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369683_comment'></div>派分脉散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369683_comment'></div>清浅数里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369683_comment'></div>汇归于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369683_comment'></div>石壁峭绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369683_comment'></div>泉流其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369683_comment'></div>信乎精气之所回复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369683_comment'></div>风雨之所蓄泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369683_comment'></div>邦人敬享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369683_comment'></div>相传名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369683_comment'></div>并山北下二十馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369683_comment'></div>有望祀之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369683_comment'></div>祠宇以神之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369683_comment'></div>蘋蘩以荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369683_comment'></div>祈农望岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369683_comment'></div>于是乎在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369683_comment'></div>祀之丰约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369683_comment'></div>在德之轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369683_comment'></div>报之迟速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369683_comment'></div>视诚之薄厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369683_comment'></div>大夫李公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369683_comment'></div>理江西三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369683_comment'></div>宽仁清净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369683_comment'></div>正德利用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369683_comment'></div>以黄韩笃厚之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369683_comment'></div>易吴楚剽轻之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369683_comment'></div>里闾之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369683_comment'></div>歌颂相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369683_comment'></div>岁在丁卯六月大旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369683_comment'></div>公勤身焦思所以救之之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369683_comment'></div>撰日洁诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369683_comment'></div>有事于神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369683_comment'></div>斋心夕往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369683_comment'></div>舣舳宵济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369683_comment'></div>厥明至于山下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369683_comment'></div>达于祠宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369683_comment'></div>精诚旁魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369683_comment'></div>灵贶交感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369683_comment'></div>通山泽之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369683_comment'></div>致阴阳之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369683_comment'></div>和气薰然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369683_comment'></div>蒸为时雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369683_comment'></div>未彻奠而繁阴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369683_comment'></div>不崇朝而甘液遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369683_comment'></div>荡洒疵疠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369683_comment'></div>布之休和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369683_comment'></div>自时厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369683_comment'></div>庶徵咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369683_comment'></div>茂遂生物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369683_comment'></div>登成甫田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369683_comment'></div>而所治七诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369683_comment'></div>如公之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369683_comment'></div>各修其封内之祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369683_comment'></div>化彼灾沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369683_comment'></div>为釐为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369683_comment'></div>其或散为祥风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369683_comment'></div>结为卿云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369683_comment'></div>纷纶葳蕤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369683_comment'></div>奔走来告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369683_comment'></div>繇是九江之西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369683_comment'></div>岁用大穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369683_comment'></div>昔董仲舒推阴阳启闭之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369683_comment'></div>相区区江都之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369683_comment'></div>用无饥年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369683_comment'></div>前史书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369683_comment'></div>况我公察廉八郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369683_comment'></div>政成化洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369683_comment'></div>人有顽薄之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369683_comment'></div>以诚革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369683_comment'></div>岁有水旱之沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369683_comment'></div>以德胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1369683_comment'></div>庶富斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1369683_comment'></div>如此之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369683_comment'></div>春秋时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369683_comment'></div>国有史氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1369683_comment'></div>君举必书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1369683_comment'></div>德舆从事于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1369683_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1369683", 1369683, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>记事</span>之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369683_comment'></div>以公之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369683_comment'></div>池之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1369683_comment'></div>明德参会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1369683_comment'></div>若合符节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1369683_comment'></div>是用追琢岩石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1369683_comment'></div>俾邦人识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1369683_comment'></div>时贞元三年八月庚子记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_90_1369683_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=787&endYear=787')">787年12月</a>　九月，外舅崔造卒。十二月初，作文祭之。作品：祭外舅相国安平公文。<div id='poem_1369817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369817?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭外舅相国安平公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（787年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369817")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369817_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369817'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369817'>维贞元三年岁次丁卯十二月朔。子婿试大理评事摄监察御史权某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369817_comment'></div>谨以清酌庶羞之奠。敬祭于外舅故相右庶子安平公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369817_comment'></div>元精熙熙。大化沄沄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369817_comment'></div>合散万形。以陶以钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369817_comment'></div>感和合祥。则生凤麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369817_comment'></div>含粹炳灵。乃有仁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369817_comment'></div>呜呼安平。受天清淳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369817_comment'></div>全德不器。大方无垠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369817_comment'></div>恭闻稚岁。卓尔殊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369817_comment'></div>亦既冠字。确乎其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369817_comment'></div>去华务实。探幽索秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369817_comment'></div>穷尽化源。深入精义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369817_comment'></div>上下千古。周流百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369817_comment'></div>自观灵龟。不嗅骄饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369817_comment'></div>考古立言。其文焕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369817_comment'></div>乃论皇极。乃志元德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369817_comment'></div>识洞窈冥。言经邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369817_comment'></div>幽兰在林。鸣鹤在阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369817_comment'></div>嘹唳芳芬。越自重深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369817_comment'></div>安贞用晦。其道乃大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369817_comment'></div>卷舒之閒。律吕相会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369817_comment'></div>相会者何。时惟赞皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369817_comment'></div>受命开府。作藩东方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369817_comment'></div>美公德辉。闇然而章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369817_comment'></div>车乘翘翘。重礼以将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369817_comment'></div>连茹时贤。是集是翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369817_comment'></div>禺禺卬卬。萃于公堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369817_comment'></div>古之待士。惧其不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369817_comment'></div>故宾不自贱。而主不自贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369817_comment'></div>道薄俗醨。其风寖隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369817_comment'></div>苟于所以。又患失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369817_comment'></div>故戟户益尊。荜户益卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369817_comment'></div>名节不立。廉隅以亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369817_comment'></div>公之出处。时之准的。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369817_comment'></div>訚訚直词。婉婉嘉画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369817_comment'></div>赞皇为主。安平为客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369817_comment'></div>化被句吴。几于耻格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369817_comment'></div>令德孔昭。触邪登朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369817_comment'></div>或塞或通。不磷不凋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369817_comment'></div>乃补衮职。柔嘉刚克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369817_comment'></div>右掖既言。其词则直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369817_comment'></div>直方明谟。与古为徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369817_comment'></div>以直言为己任。愿致君于黄虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369817_comment'></div>屡封皂囊。亦伏青蒲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369817_comment'></div>爰启爰沃。乃咨乃俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369817_comment'></div>群墨恶白。行吟楚泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369817_comment'></div>岁久逾芳。剖符建阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369817_comment'></div>政和用易。邦人乐康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369817_comment'></div>兴元之初。王旅未振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369817_comment'></div>或任专征。且迷大顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369817_comment'></div>区区遐方。独抗忠愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369817_comment'></div>驰书激切。诮喻方镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369817_comment'></div>飞章閒道。旁午奔问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369817_comment'></div>密疏安危。以扶皇运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369817_comment'></div>翠华旋宫。驰驿命公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369817_comment'></div>选部为郎。郁郁清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369817_comment'></div>克厌帝心。给事于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369817_comment'></div>乃赞大政。以釐百工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369817_comment'></div>谓俾元元。既庶而富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369817_comment'></div>未展缉熙。遽罹沈痼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369817_comment'></div>移疾请告。乞身抗疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369817_comment'></div>留中久之。不忍其去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369817_comment'></div>乃相东朝。礼备优贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369817_comment'></div>方冀勿药。再持化权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369817_comment'></div>苍苍者何。不锡永年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369817_comment'></div>寿屈其才。从古以然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369817_comment'></div>内惟小子。倥蒙褊吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369817_comment'></div>昔岁羁牵。遇公于信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369817_comment'></div>亭伯直道。君山佐郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369817_comment'></div>莫际波澜。幸窥墙仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369817_comment'></div>因曰世与道交丧。恬与智相养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369817_comment'></div>盍晦而明。盍性而情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369817_comment'></div>虚中蹈道。以此为经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369817_comment'></div>亦既归止。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1369817", 1369817, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>贫居</span>练水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369817_comment'></div>静守绪言。期于没齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369817_comment'></div>芳讯忽至。开缄盈耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369817_comment'></div>申以嘉姻。眷同国士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1369817_comment'></div>心合义固。尺书而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1369817_comment'></div>礼异常情。感深知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369817_comment'></div>音徽相继。封壤或殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369817_comment'></div>迨前年之中春。获结甘于杨都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1369817_comment'></div>夙承师友。载反门闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1369817_comment'></div>阻拜礼于上国。承施衿于外姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1369817_comment'></div>九江之西。谬见羁束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369817_comment'></div>惠爱则深。格言相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369817_comment'></div>固穷难进。是导是勖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1369817_comment'></div>心知善诱。力有不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1369817_comment'></div>一旷清德。七年于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1369817_comment'></div>物类形留。神交坐驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1369817_comment'></div>亦谓恬旷。渐消疠疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1369817_comment'></div>不虞不图。凶讣来斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1369817_comment'></div>哀激中肠。浃于四支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1369817_comment'></div>恨情礼之未展。痛幽冥之永辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1369817_comment'></div>藐彼二连。栾栾孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1369817_comment'></div>德以遗后。魂无不之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1369817_comment'></div>东洛西江。支离拘限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1369817_comment'></div>迹滞幕庭。心驰祖奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1369817_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。贤人之生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1369817_comment'></div>力命难并。年中身兮道未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1369817_comment'></div>去昭昭兮即冥冥。一往不复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1369817_comment'></div>空留淑声。衔酸托辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1369817_comment'></div>庶达明灵。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1369817_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1369817_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=787&endYear=787')">787年</a>　致书诗僧皎然，索其文辞。二十日，皎然托元判官报书，荐灵澈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=788&endYear=788')">788年5月</a>　五月，在南昌送诗僧灵澈归沃州。作品：送灵澈上人庐山回归沃洲序。<div id='poem_1369659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送灵澈上人庐山回归沃洲序</a><span class='authorDate'>（788年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369659")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369659'>昔庐山远公。钟山约公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369659_comment'></div>皆以文章广心地。用赞后学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369659_comment'></div>俾学者乘理以诣。因言而悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369659_comment'></div>得非元津之一派乎。吴兴长老昼公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369659_comment'></div>掇六义之清英。首冠方外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369659_comment'></div>入其室者。有沃洲灵澈上人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369659_comment'></div>上人心冥空无。而迹寄文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369659_comment'></div>故语甚夷易。如不出常境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369659_comment'></div>而诸生思虑。终不可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369659_comment'></div>其变也。如风松相韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369659_comment'></div>冰玉相叩。层峰千仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369659_comment'></div>下有金碧。耸鄙夫之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369659_comment'></div>初不敢视。三复则淡然天和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369659_comment'></div>晦于其中。故睹其容览其词者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369659_comment'></div>知其心不待境静而静。况会稽山水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369659_comment'></div>自古绝胜。东晋逸民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369659_comment'></div>多遗身世于此。夏五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369659_comment'></div>上人自炉峰言旋。复于是邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369659_comment'></div>予知夫拂方袍。坐轻舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369659_comment'></div>溯沿镜中。静得佳句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369659_comment'></div>然后深入空寂。万虑洗然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369659_comment'></div>则向之境物。又其稊稗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369659_comment'></div>鄙人方景慕企尚之不暇。焉敢以离群为叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369659_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1369659_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='57ac60829e60499fb3b7822072369b01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("57ac60829e60499fb3b7822072369b01");'><span id='57ac60829e60499fb3b7822072369b01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=790&endYear=790')">790年</a>，32岁</div><div id='57ac60829e60499fb3b7822072369b01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=790&endYear=790')">790年3月</a>　三月，服阕还江西，与幕府同僚游龙沙熊氏清风亭。作品：暮春陪诸公游龙沙熊氏清风亭诗序。<div id='poem_1369601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369601?labeling=true' target='_blank'>暮春陪诸公游龙沙熊氏清风亭诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（790年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369601")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369601'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369601'>暮春三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369601_comment'></div>时物具举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369601_comment'></div>先师<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1369601", 1369601, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>达贤</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369601_comment'></div>或风于舞雩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369601_comment'></div>或禊于兰亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369601_comment'></div>所以畅性灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369601_comment'></div>涤劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369601_comment'></div>使神王道胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369601_comment'></div>冥夫天倪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369601_comment'></div>吾徒束支体于府署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369601_comment'></div>以簿书为拲梏有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369601_comment'></div>故因休沐之暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369601_comment'></div>考近郊之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369601_comment'></div>郭北五里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369601_comment'></div>有古龙沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369601_comment'></div>龙沙北下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369601_comment'></div>有州人秀才熊氏清风亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369601_comment'></div>盖故容州牧戴幼公前仓部郎萧元植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369601_comment'></div>贤熊氏之业文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369601_comment'></div>尚兹境之幽旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369601_comment'></div>合资以构之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369601_comment'></div>创名以识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369601_comment'></div>五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369601_comment'></div>初入环堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369601_comment'></div>中有琴书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369601_comment'></div>披篁跻石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369601_comment'></div>忽至兹地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369601_comment'></div>鄱章二江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369601_comment'></div>分派于趾下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369601_comment'></div>匡庐群峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369601_comment'></div>极目于枕上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369601_comment'></div>或澄波净绿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369601_comment'></div>相与无际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369601_comment'></div>或孤烟归云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369601_comment'></div>明灭变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369601_comment'></div>耳目所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369601_comment'></div>异乎人寰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369601_comment'></div>志士得之为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1369601", 1369601, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>道机</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369601_comment'></div>诗人得之为佳句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369601_comment'></div>而主人生于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369601_comment'></div>习于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369601_comment'></div>其修身学文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369601_comment'></div>固加于人一等矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369601_comment'></div>况其志励于萤雪之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369601_comment'></div>业成于薪水之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369601_comment'></div>则甲科令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369601_comment'></div>如在指顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369601_comment'></div>是会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369601_comment'></div>有御史府杨君薛君环列崔君校理魏君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369601_comment'></div>皆以文发身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369601_comment'></div>或再战再克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369601_comment'></div>予与皇甫君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369601_comment'></div>不繇是进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369601_comment'></div>亦陪其欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369601_comment'></div>虚中旷然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369601_comment'></div>取乐名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369601_comment'></div>而主人趋隅拜下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369601_comment'></div>敬恭得礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369601_comment'></div>请酌古道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369601_comment'></div>遍徵歌诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369601_comment'></div>因曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369601_comment'></div>自十数年间佐是府者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369601_comment'></div>腾陵杳冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369601_comment'></div>离会靡常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369601_comment'></div>众君子用牵乎时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369601_comment'></div>未始有极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369601_comment'></div>然异日之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369601_comment'></div>非今日之适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369601_comment'></div>至若心同于内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369601_comment'></div>迹吻于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369601_comment'></div>交臂瞪视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369601_comment'></div>吾丧我于此亭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369601_comment'></div>一生几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369601_comment'></div>是不可以不纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369601_comment'></div>乃次诗于屋壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369601_comment'></div>各疏爵里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369601_comment'></div>以为清风亭故事云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_76_1369601_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安（长安）
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年1月</a>　正月，始至京师。十四日任职，散官为将仕郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年6月25日</a>　六月二十五日转左补阙，散官如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年8月</a>　八月，上疏论江淮水灾。作品：论江淮水灾上疏。<div id='poem_1369516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论江淮水灾上疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（792年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1369516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369516'>八月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369516_comment'></div>将仕●85B1守左补阙臣权德舆谨昧死顿首上疏皇帝陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369516_comment'></div>臣闻书曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369516_comment'></div>百僚师师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369516_comment'></div>百工惟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369516_comment'></div>又曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369516_comment'></div>理乱在庶官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369516_comment'></div>然则献替之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369516_comment'></div>任当耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369516_comment'></div>所以达下人之利病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369516_comment'></div>广君上之聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369516_comment'></div>惟野人炙背之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369516_comment'></div>齐士九九之贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369516_comment'></div>奖其诚心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369516_comment'></div>不致于罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369516_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下以大中大和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369516_comment'></div>武功文德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369516_comment'></div>亭育天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369516_comment'></div>十有四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369516_comment'></div>车书所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369516_comment'></div>声教大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369516_comment'></div>微臣生逢明代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369516_comment'></div>官忝谏曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369516_comment'></div>既当不讳之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369516_comment'></div>敢陈无隐之直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369516_comment'></div>伏以人为邦本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369516_comment'></div>食为人天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369516_comment'></div>或阴阳之候暂愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369516_comment'></div>水旱之沴小至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369516_comment'></div>匹夫匹妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369516_comment'></div>未安其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369516_comment'></div>纳隍之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369516_comment'></div>则有所轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369516_comment'></div>臣伏见自去年六月已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369516_comment'></div>关东多雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369516_comment'></div>淮南浙西徐蔡襄鄂等道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369516_comment'></div>霖潦为灾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369516_comment'></div>二十馀州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369516_comment'></div>皆浸没田畴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369516_comment'></div>毁败庐舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369516_comment'></div>而濒淮之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369516_comment'></div>为害特甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369516_comment'></div>因风鼓涛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369516_comment'></div>人多垫溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369516_comment'></div>其所存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369516_comment'></div>生业半空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369516_comment'></div>江东诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369516_comment'></div>业在田亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369516_comment'></div>每一岁善熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369516_comment'></div>则旁资数道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369516_comment'></div>春雨连夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369516_comment'></div>农功不开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369516_comment'></div>人心既骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369516_comment'></div>亡者则众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369516_comment'></div>幸者京师岁稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369516_comment'></div>夏麦又登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369516_comment'></div>诚为根本之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369516_comment'></div>以保斯箱之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369516_comment'></div>然赋取所资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369516_comment'></div>漕挽所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369516_comment'></div>军国大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369516_comment'></div>仰于江淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369516_comment'></div>以陛下忧劳万务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369516_comment'></div>励精为理之若是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369516_comment'></div>而天灾尚至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369516_comment'></div>将使陛下圣虑日新又日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369516_comment'></div>而儆戒之耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369516_comment'></div>不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369516_comment'></div>臣所未喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369516_comment'></div>诚灾不胜德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369516_comment'></div>赋有定制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369516_comment'></div>倘又留圣念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369516_comment'></div>因而拯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369516_comment'></div>斯实代天理物为人父母之明徵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369516_comment'></div>伏望与元老台司定议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369516_comment'></div>速下德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369516_comment'></div>遣使臣之有明识通方者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1369516_comment'></div>将恤隐之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1369516_comment'></div>尽劳徕之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369516_comment'></div>访其疾苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369516_comment'></div>蠲其租入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1369516_comment'></div>与连帅守长讲求所宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1369516_comment'></div>鳏寡幼艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1369516_comment'></div>周知其病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369516_comment'></div>诏令所下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369516_comment'></div>自如丰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1369516_comment'></div>休嘉感通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1369516_comment'></div>疵疠销散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1369516_comment'></div>况赋无工拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1369516_comment'></div>加取于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1369516_comment'></div>不若藏于人之为固也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1369516_comment'></div>盍俾有司析量入之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1369516_comment'></div>节经用之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1369516_comment'></div>务求便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1369516_comment'></div>以去冗费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1369516_comment'></div>纵灾害不甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1369516_comment'></div>陛下过而忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1369516_comment'></div>无乃益圣德之光大乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1369516_comment'></div>元元皇帝之三宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1369516_comment'></div>曰慈曰俭曰德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1369516_comment'></div>明皇帝之昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1369516_comment'></div>曰在知人在安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1369516_comment'></div>此陛下已行之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1369516_comment'></div>在恒久而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1369516_comment'></div>在敦固之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1369516_comment'></div>臣每读汉书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1369516_comment'></div>至贾谊谷永之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1369516_comment'></div>数陈理道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1369516_comment'></div>痛言得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1369516_comment'></div>汉朝不以受之为贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1369516_comment'></div>数子不以言之为罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1369516_comment'></div>我太宗文皇帝之有天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1369516_comment'></div>魏徵王圭等危言正词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1369516_comment'></div>上裨大化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1369516_comment'></div>无疆之祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1369516_comment'></div>实兆于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1369516_comment'></div>伏惟陛下远览西汉之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1369516_comment'></div>近师文皇之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1369516_comment'></div>则凡百臣庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1369516_comment'></div>敢尽其词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1369516_comment'></div>臣鄙贱顽固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1369516_comment'></div>不识忌讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1369516_comment'></div>既窃官命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1369516_comment'></div>岂敢爱身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1369516_comment'></div>盖有所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1369516_comment'></div>则合上献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1369516_comment'></div>虽蹈鼎镬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1369516_comment'></div>犹生之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1369516_comment'></div>不胜恳款惶恐之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1369516_comment'></div>伏惟陛下裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1369516_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_130_1369516_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年</a>　柳宗元以行卷来谒，数日后复温卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年11月12日</a>　十一月十二日，上疏论裴延龄之奸。作品：论度支疏。<div id='poem_1369519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论度支疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（792年11月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369519")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369519'>十一月十二日。将仕郎守右补阙臣权德舆谨昧死顿首上疏皇帝陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369519_comment'></div>臣闻建官惟贤。任人以器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369519_comment'></div>细大毕效。辕辐无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369519_comment'></div>盖就其所长。以求至当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369519_comment'></div>古人所以有忧于赵魏而劣于滕薛。败于栗邑而理于频阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369519_comment'></div>诚才各有所极也。伏见司农少卿权判度支裴延龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369519_comment'></div>早以文学。累居官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369519_comment'></div>固而似守。刻而少通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369519_comment'></div>徒有专谨之心。且非适时之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369519_comment'></div>往者贰大农之卿长。司太仓之出纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369519_comment'></div>号为称职。盖有恒规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369519_comment'></div>陛下急于奖能。切于赏善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369519_comment'></div>权委邦赋。冀有成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369519_comment'></div>且度支所务。天下至重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369519_comment'></div>量入为出。从古所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369519_comment'></div>使物无遗利而不可竭。竭则害生类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369519_comment'></div>使奸无隐情而不可刻。刻则伤人和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369519_comment'></div>调其盈虚。制其损益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369519_comment'></div>上系邦本。下系元元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369519_comment'></div>苟非全才通识。则有所壅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369519_comment'></div>自延龄受任。已近半载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369519_comment'></div>群议纷然。皆曰非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369519_comment'></div>且权其轻重。固与守之之才不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369519_comment'></div>边储经费之功。懋迁移用之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369519_comment'></div>贵无留事。以酌乎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369519_comment'></div>簿领简书。周行郡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369519_comment'></div>失于毫釐。利病相万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369519_comment'></div>一物未理。所轸皇情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369519_comment'></div>而延龄切于感恩。昧于量力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369519_comment'></div>思有以效。强所不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369519_comment'></div>则有枉尺直寻之心。多方自固之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369519_comment'></div>吏伺其隙。人售其奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369519_comment'></div>因缘蒙蔽。触类滋长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369519_comment'></div>致远恐泥。学制实伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369519_comment'></div>异时其败。罪之何补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369519_comment'></div>伏料圣意。久未正授延龄职名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369519_comment'></div>似观其能否。以为进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369519_comment'></div>官司闾里。众口一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369519_comment'></div>评议諠哗。所不可遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369519_comment'></div>伏望与一二宰臣时有裁议。或诏问度支郎官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369519_comment'></div>使得以事实条对。苟言者谬妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369519_comment'></div>盖有以辩之。或才实未称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369519_comment'></div>恐难久处。倘择能代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369519_comment'></div>命以他官。以全延龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369519_comment'></div>以便天下。上副求理之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369519_comment'></div>下遂陈力之宜。则事任交修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369519_comment'></div>职业不废。臣忝备员陛下谏诤之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369519_comment'></div>常服师训。缄默自负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369519_comment'></div>无以为容。阮嗣宗口不言人之短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369519_comment'></div>臣心常师之。但以束带立朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369519_comment'></div>则异于是。职当献纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369519_comment'></div>岂敢顾身。耳有所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369519_comment'></div>目有所见。义在无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369519_comment'></div>以奉圣明。言而获戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369519_comment'></div>臣之死所。不胜愚瞽悃款之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369519_comment'></div>伏惟陛下裁择。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369519_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1369519_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=793&endYear=793')">793年6月</a>　六月，上疏再论裴延龄不宜判度支。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年3月</a>　三月，作文祭韩洄，为撰行状。时散官已迁征事郎。作品：祭故韩祭酒文；太中大夫守国子祭酒颍川县开国男赐紫金鱼袋赠户部尚书韩公行状。<div id='poem_1369823' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369823' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369823?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭韩祭酒文</a><span class='authorDate'>（794年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369823")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369823_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369823'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369823'>维贞元十年岁次甲戌三月朔日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369823_comment'></div>徵事郎守左补阙权德舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369823_comment'></div>谨以清酌庶羞之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369823_comment'></div>敬祭于故国子祭酒韩十四丈之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369823_comment'></div>伏惟德厚流光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369823_comment'></div>炳灵发祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369823_comment'></div>传庆于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369823_comment'></div>郁为圭璋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369823_comment'></div>宣力中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369823_comment'></div>道光明代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369823_comment'></div>动必有裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369823_comment'></div>直而无悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369823_comment'></div>从容谏垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369823_comment'></div>密勿丝言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369823_comment'></div>炳然宪章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369823_comment'></div>润色化源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369823_comment'></div>天官之贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369823_comment'></div>京剧之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369823_comment'></div>四方取则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369823_comment'></div>九赋不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369823_comment'></div>蓬山秘书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369823_comment'></div>大学尊儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369823_comment'></div>选重前代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369823_comment'></div>非贤勿居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369823_comment'></div>率是明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369823_comment'></div>便藩右职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369823_comment'></div>宣其馨香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369823_comment'></div>昭其物则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369823_comment'></div>四科难并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369823_comment'></div>全才乃克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369823_comment'></div>利用无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369823_comment'></div>沛然馀力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369823_comment'></div>再世金铉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369823_comment'></div>确乎匪躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369823_comment'></div>光辅帝道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369823_comment'></div>是为门风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369823_comment'></div>缁衣棣华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369823_comment'></div>宜复于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369823_comment'></div>终缺人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369823_comment'></div>天乎不佣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369823_comment'></div>顾惟小子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369823_comment'></div>夙承先友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369823_comment'></div>骨肉之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369823_comment'></div>岁寒逾久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369823_comment'></div>爰自龆丱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369823_comment'></div>深仁善诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369823_comment'></div>恤此残生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369823_comment'></div>均其所有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369823_comment'></div>衣而食之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369823_comment'></div>禄而仕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369823_comment'></div>阖门仰给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369823_comment'></div>纤悉无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369823_comment'></div>仁恻之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369823_comment'></div>曲尽其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369823_comment'></div>二十年閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369823_comment'></div>完安保持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369823_comment'></div>比肩多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369823_comment'></div>忝迹清时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369823_comment'></div>必由念虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369823_comment'></div>敢不知思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369823_comment'></div>秦原苍苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369823_comment'></div>丹旐迟迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369823_comment'></div>精魂何往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369823_comment'></div>音容莫追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369823_comment'></div>沈哀激中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369823_comment'></div>雪涕交挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369823_comment'></div>神鉴如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369823_comment'></div>含酸托词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369823_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1369823_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年4月28日</a>　四月二十八日，迁起居舍人，由奚陟荐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年</a>　刘禹锡致书，呈近作十余篇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年8月21日</a>　八月二十一日，兼知制诰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年10月3日</a>　十月三日，奉诏主考制科，擢贤良方正、能直言极谏十七人，裴度为首。<br /><a href="javascript: "poem_title_1369841")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369841'>维贞元十一年岁次乙亥十月朔日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369841_comment'></div>子婿起居舍人知制诰权某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369841_comment'></div>谨以清酌庶羞之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369841_comment'></div>敬祭于外姑故河东县君之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369841_comment'></div>伏惟承积德之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369841_comment'></div>禀醇仁之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369841_comment'></div>嫔于盛门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369841_comment'></div>播此淑行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369841_comment'></div>恭闻幼仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369841_comment'></div>以及结缡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369841_comment'></div>居然绸直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369841_comment'></div>不待姆师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369841_comment'></div>朝尊相府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369841_comment'></div>家荣命妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369841_comment'></div>琴瑟和声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369841_comment'></div>珩璜节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369841_comment'></div>执谦处约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369841_comment'></div>不改其素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369841_comment'></div>专静是宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369841_comment'></div>纷华靡务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369841_comment'></div>四德日滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369841_comment'></div>六姻是宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369841_comment'></div>睦亲以诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369841_comment'></div>抚下以慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369841_comment'></div>内则之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369841_comment'></div>采蘩之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369841_comment'></div>夙夜无违。<div id='poem_sentence_33_1369841_comment'></div>方庆䌽衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369841_comment'></div>遽惊丧服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369841_comment'></div>顾惟鄙人。<div id='poem_sentence_38_1369841_comment'></div>情以理亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369841_comment'></div>顷岁违阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369841_comment'></div>遐方食贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369841_comment'></div>残生未灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369841_comment'></div>慰训相循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369841_comment'></div>俄忝周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369841_comment'></div>来归帝里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369841_comment'></div>驱车遄迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369841_comment'></div>尽室至止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369841_comment'></div>举觞为寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369841_comment'></div>侍坐以齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369841_comment'></div>令节游娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369841_comment'></div>温颜燕喜。<div
