id='poem_sentence_53_1369841_comment'></div>遽此全归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369841_comment'></div>难徵神理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369841_comment'></div>栾栾棘人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369841_comment'></div>泣奉涂刍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369841_comment'></div>翩翩素旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369841_comment'></div>东指洛都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369841_comment'></div>征途在目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369841_comment'></div>官局所拘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369841_comment'></div>含凄国门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369841_comment'></div>拜奠路隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369841_comment'></div>仁爱如昨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369841_comment'></div>幽明忽殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369841_comment'></div>托词写哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369841_comment'></div>庶达泉垆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369841_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1369841_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年11月21日</a>　十一月二十一日，改尚书省驾部员外郎，仍知制诰。散官迁宣德郎，勋官为云骑尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=796&endYear=796')">796年</a>　在驾部员外郎任、知制诰。与同僚祭李泌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年</a>　在驾部员外郎任，充进士试策官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年8月</a>　八月，独孤及子郁有书来谒，答之甚眷。作品：答独孤秀才书。<div id='poem_1369585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369585?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答独孤秀才书</a><span class='authorDate'>（797年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369585")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369585'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369585'>省四日书问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369585_comment'></div>兼示新文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369585_comment'></div>闳博峻异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369585_comment'></div>有立言致远之旨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369585_comment'></div>其于惠爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369585_comment'></div>纤悉厚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369585_comment'></div>甚善甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369585_comment'></div>以吾子才志与年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369585_comment'></div>三者皆当以家声自振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369585_comment'></div>若建瓴决水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369585_comment'></div>大冶良工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369585_comment'></div>必有不期至而至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369585_comment'></div>况以日日新又日新之盛哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369585_comment'></div>夫豫章珠玑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369585_comment'></div>镆铘毛嫱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369585_comment'></div>终不虑隐之椟之襓之帷之之为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369585_comment'></div>而为拥肿砾石铅钝宿瘤之排蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369585_comment'></div>但发有疾徐耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369585_comment'></div>来问云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369585_comment'></div>一人惊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369585_comment'></div>亦已多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369585_comment'></div>岂与族凡校耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369585_comment'></div>此诚得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369585_comment'></div>又云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369585_comment'></div>先达病不能公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369585_comment'></div>或公而不能甚力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369585_comment'></div>今夫滔滔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369585_comment'></div>或辩之不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369585_comment'></div>而苟善待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369585_comment'></div>及扬声延誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369585_comment'></div>则钳口结舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369585_comment'></div>大凡举世之病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369585_comment'></div>如鄙夫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369585_comment'></div>直力不足耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369585_comment'></div>亦惧招徕奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369585_comment'></div>为津为岐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369585_comment'></div>至有窃所爱者则寡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369585_comment'></div>又岂能废是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369585_comment'></div>从古未达者之望达者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369585_comment'></div>何尝不如是耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369585_comment'></div>先师七十子所拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369585_comment'></div>岂敢当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369585_comment'></div>三复戁然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369585_comment'></div>无言喻怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369585_comment'></div>其他慕重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369585_comment'></div>续俟会话。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369585_comment'></div>德舆顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1369585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年4月1日</a>　四月一日，迁尚书司勋郎中，兼知制诰，散官为朝议郎，赐绯鱼袋，勋官如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　上昭陵寝宫奏议。作品：昭陵寝宫议。<div id='poem_1369575' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369575' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369575?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭陵寝宫议<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369575")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369575_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1369575_0'>① 右奉进止寝宫在山上置来多年曾野火烧爇摧毁略尽其宫寻移在瑶台寺左侧今属通年欲议修置缘旧宫本在山上元无井泉每缘供水稍远百姓非常劳弊今欲于见住行宫处修造所冀久远便人又为改移旧制恐所见未周宜令中书门下及百寮同商量可否闻奏</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369575'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369575'>朝议郎守尚书司勋郎中知制诰云骑尉赐绯鱼袋臣权德舆议曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369575_comment'></div>臣闻古宗庙之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369575_comment'></div>前有庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369575_comment'></div>庙列昭穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369575_comment'></div>后有寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369575_comment'></div>寝陈衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369575_comment'></div>自秦汉已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369575_comment'></div>始因陵立庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369575_comment'></div>有寝宫便殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369575_comment'></div>虽庙居陵旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369575_comment'></div>而无必在山上不在山下之定制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369575_comment'></div>且礼文所贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369575_comment'></div>宜也称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369575_comment'></div>祀事所资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369575_comment'></div>敬也洁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369575_comment'></div>伏以昭陵因山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369575_comment'></div>太宗所建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369575_comment'></div>宫在山上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369575_comment'></div>以便当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369575_comment'></div>自野火延烧行宫山下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369575_comment'></div>亦已久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369575_comment'></div>今若伐木缩板。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369575_comment'></div>程功就险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369575_comment'></div>神道贵静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369575_comment'></div>或非所宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369575_comment'></div>则与置陵之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369575_comment'></div>事体为异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369575_comment'></div>况旧制既毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369575_comment'></div>新宫是修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369575_comment'></div>考于便地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369575_comment'></div>可以经久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369575_comment'></div>所谓宜称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369575_comment'></div>又井泉在下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369575_comment'></div>汲引为易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369575_comment'></div>享献之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369575_comment'></div>是资严恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369575_comment'></div>本于明德惟馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369575_comment'></div>亦在吉蠲为饎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369575_comment'></div>故礼之言祭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369575_comment'></div>水曰清涤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369575_comment'></div>言其洁清涤濯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369575_comment'></div>又曰不敢用常亵味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369575_comment'></div>所以交于神明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369575_comment'></div>因兹列井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369575_comment'></div>以备荐羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369575_comment'></div>所谓洁而敬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369575_comment'></div>凡举事必以制度当否为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369575_comment'></div>而以人力劳逸为细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369575_comment'></div>若于事为当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369575_comment'></div>又无所劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369575_comment'></div>不亦顺昭陵爱人之心乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369575_comment'></div>不亦叶陛下从宜之礼乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369575_comment'></div>今列圣寝宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369575_comment'></div>有在山下者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369575_comment'></div>然则致敬来格之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369575_comment'></div>岂以山上山下为远近耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369575_comment'></div>臣愚以为但在柏城之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369575_comment'></div>则不云远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369575_comment'></div>陛下精诚慎重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369575_comment'></div>询及庶僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369575_comment'></div>徒献所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369575_comment'></div>伏增战越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369575_comment'></div>谨议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1369575_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=799&endYear=799')">799年</a>　冬月，擢中书舍人，勋散赐如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年1月</a>　正月，上《淮西招讨事宜》<div id='poem_1369564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369564?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淮西招讨事宜状</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369564")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369564'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369564'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369564_comment'></div>自去岁出师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369564_comment'></div>今已周月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369564_comment'></div>军威未振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369564_comment'></div>寇孽犹虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369564_comment'></div>中外臣庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369564_comment'></div>实同愤切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369564_comment'></div>臣伏思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369564_comment'></div>以王命讨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1369564", 1369564, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>不庭</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369564_comment'></div>以平天下师临区区淮西之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369564_comment'></div>况申光褊小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369564_comment'></div>惟有蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369564_comment'></div>以宗社威灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369564_comment'></div>睿谋上略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369564_comment'></div>所宜朝出令而夕献捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369564_comment'></div>乘城授首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369564_comment'></div>指顾可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369564_comment'></div>今胜负之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369564_comment'></div>犹未相直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369564_comment'></div>师老财废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369564_comment'></div>劳而无功者何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369564_comment'></div>盖有以也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369564_comment'></div>以寇之乘乱专地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369564_comment'></div>已十五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369564_comment'></div>财征不至于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369564_comment'></div>杼轴难资于军实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369564_comment'></div>而又峻威令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369564_comment'></div>同丰约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369564_comment'></div>兽穷则抟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369564_comment'></div>人自为战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369564_comment'></div>此皆必死之众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369564_comment'></div>以全义之忠朴果决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369564_comment'></div>固思报恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369564_comment'></div>而驭众代谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369564_comment'></div>力或不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369564_comment'></div>况山东士旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369564_comment'></div>骄悍且久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369564_comment'></div>苟非威望素重者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369564_comment'></div>岂能制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369564_comment'></div>又诸侯之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369564_comment'></div>头会乌合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369564_comment'></div>或幸灾养寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369564_comment'></div>或绵力薄材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369564_comment'></div>胜既众分其劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369564_comment'></div>败又无所归罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369564_comment'></div>其心不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369564_comment'></div>姑务自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369564_comment'></div>此非成功之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369564_comment'></div>臣以为徵师太广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369564_comment'></div>命将太轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369564_comment'></div>轻则无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369564_comment'></div>广则难制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369564_comment'></div>议者或曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369564_comment'></div>统师之名不重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369564_comment'></div>则策勋之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369564_comment'></div>其赏易足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369564_comment'></div>偏师之任不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369564_comment'></div>则劳旋之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369564_comment'></div>其功自分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369564_comment'></div>且以希烈襄阳为之惩创。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369564_comment'></div>此乃知其一而不知其二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369564_comment'></div>成功之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369564_comment'></div>在法制钤键之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369564_comment'></div>岂可早计过虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369564_comment'></div>使陷于必不成功哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369564_comment'></div>自古以兵多而败者非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369564_comment'></div>以近事则乾元邺城之围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369564_comment'></div>大历魏州之讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369564_comment'></div>非师不众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369564_comment'></div>今因其数道会师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369564_comment'></div>可以精择将帅武略威重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369564_comment'></div>为圣心所知群情所伏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369564_comment'></div>其馀方面二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369564_comment'></div>与汝邓之地环寇四境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369564_comment'></div>度其不能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369564_comment'></div>速易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369564_comment'></div>两河远地之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1369564_comment'></div>未能制其死命者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1369564_comment'></div>悉罢去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369564_comment'></div>但以便地劲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369564_comment'></div>练其可用者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1369564_comment'></div>誓以赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1369564_comment'></div>使之犄角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1369564_comment'></div>设备于要害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369564_comment'></div>同心以进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369564_comment'></div>程其力用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1369564_comment'></div>如臂使指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1369564_comment'></div>此决胜之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1369564_comment'></div>其次则严戒慎固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1369564_comment'></div>勿与争锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1369564_comment'></div>来则遏其驱侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1369564_comment'></div>去则保兹经界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1369564_comment'></div>使士勇皆贾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1369564_comment'></div>终不妄动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1369564_comment'></div>有虏获者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1369564_comment'></div>悉释而归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1369564_comment'></div>耀以武力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1369564_comment'></div>浃之恩信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1369564_comment'></div>既无馈运之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1369564_comment'></div>又无杀伐之伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1369564_comment'></div>彼竭我盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1369564_comment'></div>可以岁月待其毙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1369564_comment'></div>倘以其未有出境之暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1369564_comment'></div>且开请罪之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1369564_comment'></div>下诏班师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1369564_comment'></div>旷然全宥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1369564_comment'></div>虽根本未靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1369564_comment'></div>且罢战息人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1369564_comment'></div>又其次也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1369564_comment'></div>若止如今者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1369564_comment'></div>二十馀军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1369564_comment'></div>禁令不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1369564_comment'></div>以怀归之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1369564_comment'></div>无效命之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1369564_comment'></div>望其成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1369564_comment'></div>亦已难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1369564_comment'></div>伏惟陛下留念。</div><div id='poem_sentence_116_1369564_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年2月</a>　二月，杨于陵拜京兆少尹，为作西厅壁记。作品：京兆少尹西厅壁记。<div id='poem_1369679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>京兆少尹西厅壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369679")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369679'>汉制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369679_comment'></div>三辅丞秩六百石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369679_comment'></div>至东汉秩千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369679_comment'></div>魏晋为京兆郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369679_comment'></div>则曰治中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369679_comment'></div>至隋则曰司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369679_comment'></div>又曰赞治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369679_comment'></div>国家沿前代之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369679_comment'></div>再更其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369679_comment'></div>至开元初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369679_comment'></div>命为少尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369679_comment'></div>其员二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369679_comment'></div>其品四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369679_comment'></div>纲纪众务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369679_comment'></div>而分贰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369679_comment'></div>上助官师表则之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369679_comment'></div>而佐其慈惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369679_comment'></div>下董掾史属城之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369679_comment'></div>而推其功善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369679_comment'></div>大积而不挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369679_comment'></div>中行而有伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369679_comment'></div>和协辑睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369679_comment'></div>宣明教令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369679_comment'></div>非文行政事之全者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369679_comment'></div>不得居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369679_comment'></div>贞元十六年春二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369679_comment'></div>诏宏农杨于陵字达夫自吏部郎中莅其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369679_comment'></div>先是达夫之佐元侯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369679_comment'></div>四入御史府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369679_comment'></div>登天台也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369679_comment'></div>五为剧曹郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369679_comment'></div>懿文菁华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369679_comment'></div>履行直温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369679_comment'></div>折中宪令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369679_comment'></div>克勤细大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369679_comment'></div>是宜典司名命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369679_comment'></div>列侍左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369679_comment'></div>而犹以吏理扬历于浩穰之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369679_comment'></div>抑天之爱人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369679_comment'></div>俾覆露于毂下耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369679_comment'></div>或姑阅其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369679_comment'></div>而将大授之耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369679_comment'></div>初西厅少尹视事之堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369679_comment'></div>大历中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369679_comment'></div>其长黎氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369679_comment'></div>以胜势之近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369679_comment'></div>取为亭沼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369679_comment'></div>故移创于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369679_comment'></div>自后厥官罕备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369679_comment'></div>居之者不推本所代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369679_comment'></div>而斯宇寖废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369679_comment'></div>及达夫之拜未浃旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369679_comment'></div>其僚继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369679_comment'></div>于是达夫徵缺员以循旧常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369679_comment'></div>宏必葺以办攸处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369679_comment'></div>用宿其业而修其方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369679_comment'></div>凡所颛督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369679_comment'></div>武备厩置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369679_comment'></div>刑书纠禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369679_comment'></div>工徒启塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369679_comment'></div>三右曹之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369679_comment'></div>大凡天子县内之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369679_comment'></div>无不赞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369679_comment'></div>无不抗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369679_comment'></div>称职者或退其品而选于近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369679_comment'></div>或进其材而擢为大吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369679_comment'></div>佐六官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369679_comment'></div>分十联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369679_comment'></div>皆其迁次然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369679_comment'></div>以旧记湮落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369679_comment'></div>虑失其传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369679_comment'></div>今断自太极元年而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369679_comment'></div>列其名氏岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369679_comment'></div>俾风采相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369679_comment'></div>且为故志云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1369679_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年7月</a>　七月，为宰相郑余庆弟具瞻作秘书郎壁记。作品：秘书郎厅壁记。<div id='poem_1369678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秘书郎厅壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369678")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369678'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369678'>按六典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369678_comment'></div>秘书郎四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369678_comment'></div>从六品上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369678_comment'></div>分掌四部书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369678_comment'></div>以甲乙丙丁为之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369678_comment'></div>昔汉武帝聚天下文籍于广内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369678_comment'></div>谓之中秘书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369678_comment'></div>魏晋之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369678_comment'></div>秘书与中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369678_comment'></div>或分或合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369678_comment'></div>故云职近日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369678_comment'></div>宜居三台之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369678_comment'></div>丞郎之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369678_comment'></div>与南宫相亚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369678_comment'></div>历代辨论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369678_comment'></div>与时轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369678_comment'></div>国初思汉廷延阁之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369678_comment'></div>薄江左贵游之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369678_comment'></div>始以岑江陵虞永兴褚河南迭为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369678_comment'></div>厥后彬彬多文学之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369678_comment'></div>然则先王之法制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369678_comment'></div>官师之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1369678", 1369678, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>训典</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369678_comment'></div>九流百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369678_comment'></div>如贯珠然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369678_comment'></div>学与仕皆优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369678_comment'></div>而旋相为用者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369678_comment'></div>其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369678_comment'></div>今年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369678_comment'></div>荥阳郑君具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369678_comment'></div>自泾阳尉承诏授任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369678_comment'></div>郑君质重而有敏行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369678_comment'></div>坦夷而含明识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369678_comment'></div>且今中书相君之令弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369678_comment'></div>方以结绶满岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369678_comment'></div>调于选部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369678_comment'></div>言吏资者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369678_comment'></div>积三迁而后至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369678_comment'></div>今超居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369678_comment'></div>有以见择贤审官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369678_comment'></div>与怡怡绰绰之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369678_comment'></div>为尽美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369678_comment'></div>在晋郑默领中外三阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369678_comment'></div>始删烦文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369678_comment'></div>而朱紫不杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369678_comment'></div>开元初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369678_comment'></div>君之王考颍川府君叔祖刑部府君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369678_comment'></div>皆繇礼官博士继登其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369678_comment'></div>诸父诸兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369678_comment'></div>或解巾以司雠校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369678_comment'></div>或功次而奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369678_comment'></div>含章筮仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369678_comment'></div>多在于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369678_comment'></div>犹桓公武公之代为卿士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369678_comment'></div>盖善于其职而宜之之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369678_comment'></div>谓鄙人尝学旧史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369678_comment'></div>能知书府官业之所繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369678_comment'></div>是俾编次郎位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369678_comment'></div>彰施屋壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369678_comment'></div>时贞元庚辰秋七月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1369678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　以女归于独孤郁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　冬，以中书舍人典礼部贡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=802&endYear=802')">802年</a>　任中书舍人，放进士二十三人及第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=802&endYear=802')">802年4月</a>　四月，为宰相贾耽《贞元十道录》作序。作品：魏国公贞元十道录序。<div id='poem_1369668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>魏国公贞元十道录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（802年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369668")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369668'>序曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369668_comment'></div>自夏书禹贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369668_comment'></div>周官职方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369668_comment'></div>汉志地理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369668_comment'></div>厥后史臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369668_comment'></div>继有其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369668_comment'></div>国家将九夷丕冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369668_comment'></div>四海梯航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369668_comment'></div>声朔过前古远甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369668_comment'></div>相国魏公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369668_comment'></div>明诚助化育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369668_comment'></div>奥学穷古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369668_comment'></div>百揆师长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369668_comment'></div>十年枢衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369668_comment'></div>赞端拱无为之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369668_comment'></div>以宥天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369668_comment'></div>王佐盛业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369668_comment'></div>论著形焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369668_comment'></div>尝以为言区域者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369668_comment'></div>阔略未备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369668_comment'></div>或传疑失实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369668_comment'></div>于是献海内华夷图一轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369668_comment'></div>古今郡国县道四夷述四十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369668_comment'></div>尽瀛海之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369668_comment'></div>穷鞮译之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369668_comment'></div>陈农不获之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369668_comment'></div>朱赣未条之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369668_comment'></div>贯穿切劘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369668_comment'></div>靡不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1369668", 1369668, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>详究</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369668_comment'></div>开卷尽在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369668_comment'></div>披图朗然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369668_comment'></div>又撮其要会切于今者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369668_comment'></div>为贞元十道录四卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369668_comment'></div>其首篇自贞观初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369668_comment'></div>以天下诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369668_comment'></div>分隶十道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369668_comment'></div>随山河江岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369668_comment'></div>控带纡直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369668_comment'></div>割裂经界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369668_comment'></div>而为都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369668_comment'></div>在景云为按察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369668_comment'></div>在开元为采访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369668_comment'></div>在天宝以州为郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369668_comment'></div>在乾元复郡为州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369668_comment'></div>六典地域之差次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369668_comment'></div>四方贡职之名物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369668_comment'></div>废置升降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369668_comment'></div>提封险易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369668_comment'></div>因时制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369668_comment'></div>皆备于编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369668_comment'></div>而又考迹其疆理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369668_comment'></div>以正谬误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369668_comment'></div>采获其要害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369668_comment'></div>而陈开置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369668_comment'></div>至若护单于府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369668_comment'></div>并马邑以北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369668_comment'></div>理榆林关外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369668_comment'></div>宜隶河东乐安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369668_comment'></div>自乾元后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369668_comment'></div>河流改故道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369668_comment'></div>宜隶河南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369668_comment'></div>合川七郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369668_comment'></div>北与陇坻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369668_comment'></div>南与庸蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369668_comment'></div>回远不相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369668_comment'></div>宜于武都建都府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369668_comment'></div>以恢边备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369668_comment'></div>大凡类是者十有二条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369668_comment'></div>制万方之枢键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369668_comment'></div>出千古之耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369668_comment'></div>故今之言地理者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369668_comment'></div>称魏公焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369668_comment'></div>公之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369668_comment'></div>岂徒洽闻广记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369668_comment'></div>以学名家而已哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369668_comment'></div>盖体国远驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369668_comment'></div>不出户而知天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1369668_comment'></div>亲百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1369668_comment'></div>抚四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369668_comment'></div>真宰相之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369668_comment'></div>凡今三十一节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1369668_comment'></div>十一观察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1369668_comment'></div>与防御经略以守臣称使府者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1369668_comment'></div>共五十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369668_comment'></div>列于首篇之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369668_comment'></div>其三篇则以十道为准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1369668_comment'></div>县距州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1369668_comment'></div>州距两都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1369668_comment'></div>书其道里之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1369668_comment'></div>与其四鄙所抵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1369668_comment'></div>其事覈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1369668_comment'></div>其言详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1369668_comment'></div>闳览默识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1369668_comment'></div>精微错综。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1369668_comment'></div>斯为至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1369668_comment'></div>德舆忝掖垣之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1369668_comment'></div>承公话言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1369668_comment'></div>盱衡屈指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1369668_comment'></div>珠贯冰释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1369668_comment'></div>辱命授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1369668_comment'></div>书其大端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1369668_comment'></div>辄罄斐然之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1369668_comment'></div>岂扬不休之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1369668_comment'></div>时贞元壬午岁夏四月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1369668_comment'></div>谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_104_1369668_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=802&endYear=802')">802年10月</a>　十月，真拜礼部侍郎，勋散赐如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年</a>　任礼部侍郎，放进士二十人及第，据京兆尹李实请托。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年7月</a>　七月，因旱上疏论朝政之失。作品：论旱灾表。<div id='poem_1369565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论旱灾表</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369565")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369565'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369565'>臣德舆言。伏见自春三月不雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369565_comment'></div>连夏涉秋。田里嗷嗷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369565_comment'></div>农收无望。陛下斋心减膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369565_comment'></div>悯恻元元。告于宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369565_comment'></div>祷于天地。一物可祈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369565_comment'></div>必致其礼。一介有请者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369565_comment'></div>必诚其言。忧人闵雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369565_comment'></div>可谓至矣。而甘泽未降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369565_comment'></div>众情如焚。公私窘迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369565_comment'></div>日月以甚。臣闻水旱之沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369565_comment'></div>阴阳之变。前哲王之所不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369565_comment'></div>但有备之之术而已。销天灾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369565_comment'></div>莫若修政事。感人心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369565_comment'></div>莫若流惠泽。人和浃洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369565_comment'></div>则天地之和应矣。昔尧舜在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369565_comment'></div>天下无穷人。今陛下爱人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369565_comment'></div>远过尧舜。而犹有穷困未济者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369565_comment'></div>此臣所未喻也。敢以朴愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369565_comment'></div>条陈管见。伏惟圣虑裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369565_comment'></div>一。顷年纵旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369565_comment'></div>亦皆有苗。但时雨或愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369565_comment'></div>不秀不实。今则甸畿之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369565_comment'></div>多有不下种而不生出者。才出短苗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369565_comment'></div>旋即焦乾者。大率皆赤地而无所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369565_comment'></div>流庸转徙之人。或趍近辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369565_comment'></div>或抵京西。毙踣彫耗于道途者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369565_comment'></div>又居其外。但虑至种麦时无种可下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369565_comment'></div>顷者夏麦。所收盖寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369565_comment'></div>旋属旱歉。性命是虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369565_comment'></div>迫于目前。苟利糊口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369565_comment'></div>蚩蚩愚夫。须与支计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369565_comment'></div>伏望以今年夏税麦中。各于本县量留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369565_comment'></div>充临时赈贷麦种。今年秋税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369565_comment'></div>除水利地据分数外。馀一切放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369565_comment'></div>远年逋负。悉皆蠲除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369565_comment'></div>发德音。下明诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369565_comment'></div>沛然及物。使皆闻知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369565_comment'></div>则人心重迁。喜气交感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369565_comment'></div>假使不放。亦决无可徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369565_comment'></div>不若先事图之。则恩归于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369565_comment'></div>此乃今之至切也。去贞元十四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369565_comment'></div>夏旱不甚于今。官吏多督责取办以为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369565_comment'></div>不副陛下视人如伤之旨。至有县令为部内百姓殴击者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369565_comment'></div>前事不远。伏惟陛下留念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369565_comment'></div>一。漕运之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369565_comment'></div>以济关中。有司量入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369565_comment'></div>固以支计。以臣愚所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369565_comment'></div>且自东都以来。缘路仓所贮米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369565_comment'></div>随水陆节给。倍程般运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369565_comment'></div>应给脚价。皆与实钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369565_comment'></div>务令速到京师。不计在途省费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369565_comment'></div>续计料江淮米入运。以备恒数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369565_comment'></div>又以太仓粟。约一岁费之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369565_comment'></div>出粜于人。则时价必减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369565_comment'></div>而蓄藏者自出矣。一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369565_comment'></div>书曰。罪疑惟轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369565_comment'></div>又曰。宥过无大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369565_comment'></div>陛下已命省寺。疏理系囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369565_comment'></div>各从减等。务使原免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369565_comment'></div>此诚睿慈恤隐。莫大之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369565_comment'></div>臣愚以为不如特降成命。敷宣于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369565_comment'></div>使毂下万人。涣然受赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369565_comment'></div>又比来有经黜放者。自谓永无录用之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369565_comment'></div>坐为匪人。感动和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369565_comment'></div>冬荐官踰三年未受命者。不敢出城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369565_comment'></div>相顾以乞食。溘然而就毙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369565_comment'></div>此亦穷人之一端也。近有超擢黜放者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369565_comment'></div>或起为二千石。其徒必互相慰勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369565_comment'></div>上荷圣恩。虽未命者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369565_comment'></div>知牵复可望。冬荐官皆叙已用适其轮辕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369565_comment'></div>此诚睿慈勤虑。奖人于禄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369565_comment'></div>伏惟因而宏之。使人人自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369565_comment'></div>昔颜子不贰过。蘧伯玉知非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369565_comment'></div>则明古之贤人。皆不能无过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369565_comment'></div>在知而改之而已。弃瑕奖善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369565_comment'></div>用其所长。则无废人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369565_comment'></div>此理道之至切也。一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1369565_comment'></div>天下理在百姓安。百姓安在赋税减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1369565_comment'></div>赋税减在经费省。天下未有不由此涂出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369565_comment'></div>生之者少。靡之者多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369565_comment'></div>物力既屈。人命必蹶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1369565_comment'></div>大历中绢一疋价近四千。今止八百九百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1369565_comment'></div>设使税入之数如其旧。出于人者已五倍其多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1369565_comment'></div>又四方守臣。锐于上献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369565_comment'></div>为国敛怨。为身市恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369565_comment'></div>或广军实之求。而兵有虚籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1369565_comment'></div>或倍地征之数。而取以多方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1369565_comment'></div>固非家财皆出于人力者也。虽有心计巧历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1369565_comment'></div>能商功利者。其于困人均也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1369565_comment'></div>割股啖口。莫甚于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1369565_comment'></div>在陛下虑之而已。行之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1369565_comment'></div>大易节之说曰。天地节而四时成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1369565_comment'></div>节以制度。不伤财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1369565_comment'></div>不害人。伏望俾有司审量入之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1369565_comment'></div>节轻用之源。无冗食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1369565_comment'></div>无浮费。百事省啬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1369565_comment'></div>以俟丰年。此一救灾恤患之切务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1369565_comment'></div>一。前史云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1369565_comment'></div>一时不雨。人且狼顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1369565_comment'></div>今历三时矣。农之望岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1369565_comment'></div>以食为天。京师比屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1369565_comment'></div>惶惶靡措。诗曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1369565_comment'></div>先人有言。询于刍荛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1369565_comment'></div>古语云。愚者千虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1369565_comment'></div>时有一得。况含齿戴发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1369565_comment'></div>斯人最灵。伏望俾百执事之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1369565_comment'></div>皆得上言利病。可者酌而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1369565_comment'></div>否者容而恕之。此亦恻隐含宏之大要也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1369565_comment'></div>以前臣伏以今年饥旱。京师艰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1369565_comment'></div>圣心忧轸。臣下何安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1369565_comment'></div>臣谓救之者不在于祷求。乃在于事实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1369565_comment'></div>有备者不止于公廪。亦在于编人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1369565_comment'></div>苟怀愚管。不敢缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1369565_comment'></div>上烦宸扆。事或非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1369565_comment'></div>慺慺血诚。所贵无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1369565_comment'></div>不任惶灼陨越之至。谨稿手疏以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1369565_comment'></div>臣某诚恐诚惧顿首顿首。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1369565_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_117_1369565_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=804&endYear=804')">804年</a>　任礼部侍郎，冬，典贡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年</a>　正月，撰德宗谥册文。作品：唐德宗皇帝谥册文。<div id='poem_1369808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐德宗皇帝谥册文</a><span class='authorDate'>（805年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369808")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369808'>维永贞元年岁次乙酉十月景申朔。孝孙嗣皇帝臣某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369808_comment'></div>伏维大行皇帝德合天地。作人父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369808_comment'></div>纂承光明。建用皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369808_comment'></div>昔在宝应。制天下赋舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369808_comment'></div>戚藩以大。自鲁疏雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369808_comment'></div>师律既贞。会陕收洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369808_comment'></div>克燀威命。廓开王涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369808_comment'></div>自登上嗣。乃宅丕后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369808_comment'></div>服艺祖神宗之大烈。有乾乾翼翼之至敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369808_comment'></div>敷佑迪哲。尊严懿恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369808_comment'></div>烛明四极。发育万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369808_comment'></div>濯沐乎仁泽。澄清乎理本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369808_comment'></div>巍巍乎建中风声。与贞观同符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369808_comment'></div>洎时有祲沴。变生京毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369808_comment'></div>省方履薄。宏阴骘之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369808_comment'></div>整旅致诛。申震耀之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369808_comment'></div>氛祲灭息。侯王轨道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369808_comment'></div>丕冒持载。镜清砥平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369808_comment'></div>然后明禋毖祀。万灵以接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369808_comment'></div>翕受敷施。九德咸事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369808_comment'></div>含宏亭毒。以致其和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369808_comment'></div>博采虚受。以通其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369808_comment'></div>政刑有箴。宸扆有铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369808_comment'></div>焕乎文明之化成也。因时创节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369808_comment'></div>象卦设乐。薰然中和之被物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369808_comment'></div>纳嘉言于近侍。辍已行之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369808_comment'></div>疾谗口于宵人。宥过误之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369808_comment'></div>去徽号而约已。正庙祧而尊祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369808_comment'></div>九译通道。万方来庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369808_comment'></div>賨旅焯乎勋籍。夷歌陈于乐府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369808_comment'></div>霜露所队。车书大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369808_comment'></div>顺气旁达。天休滋至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369808_comment'></div>庆霄轮囷。德水清澈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369808_comment'></div>三辰秉阳以宣耀。百嘉丽地而交感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369808_comment'></div>飞走呈祥。肖翘遂性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369808_comment'></div>在宥天下二十有七年。夫文思光被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369808_comment'></div>陶唐之盛也。憯怛忠利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369808_comment'></div>虞帝之教也。亹亹穆穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369808_comment'></div>周文之业也。聪明神武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369808_comment'></div>汉祖之烈也。穷古先之大律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369808_comment'></div>极帝者之上仪。方将扈升介丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369808_comment'></div>侍检玉牒。奄遗天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369808_comment'></div>永弃万方。亿兆嗷嗷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369808_comment'></div>哀号靡诉。顾惟冲昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369808_comment'></div>惧忝孙谋。君父有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369808_comment'></div>付兹神器。虔恭贻训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369808_comment'></div>感慕滋深。今因山既建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369808_comment'></div>同轨毕至。一二元老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369808_comment'></div>宗工硕生。考称天之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369808_comment'></div>稽节惠之法。式遵古义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369808_comment'></div>敢荐大名。谨遣摄太尉门下侍郎平章事杜黄裳谨奉册上尊谥曰神武孝文皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369808_comment'></div>庙曰德宗。伏惟圣灵昭格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369808_comment'></div>膺是典礼。幽赞丕祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369808_comment'></div>流于无穷。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369808_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1369808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年</a>　冬，迁吏部侍郎，勋散封赐如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>　春，改太子宾客，散官迁朝议大夫，勋封赐如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　三月，复任兵部侍郎，散官迁太中大夫，勋官迁上柱国，爵封襄武县开国侯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年4月15日</a>　四月十五日，上奏论昭义军事宜。作品：昭义军事宜状。<div id='poem_1369566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭义军事宜状</a><span class='authorDate'>（809年4月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369566")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369566'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369566'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369566_comment'></div>山东节将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369566_comment'></div>有沃壤利兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369566_comment'></div>三十年间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369566_comment'></div>寖以强大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369566_comment'></div>或父殁子继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369566_comment'></div>起复临戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369566_comment'></div>名器虽出于中朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369566_comment'></div>爵地实专于外阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369566_comment'></div>泽潞素为雄镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369566_comment'></div>磁邢洺与数道犬牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369566_comment'></div>故欲变山东之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369566_comment'></div>先在择昭义之帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369566_comment'></div>可以练兵赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369566_comment'></div>循法制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369566_comment'></div>镇以威重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369566_comment'></div>扼其咽喉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369566_comment'></div>化彼诪张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369566_comment'></div>纳诸轨度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369566_comment'></div>此为枢键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369566_comment'></div>不可不慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369566_comment'></div>卢从史拔自军校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369566_comment'></div>列于藩垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369566_comment'></div>以先朝含煦之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369566_comment'></div>积臣以宠禄之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369566_comment'></div>且自建中贞元以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369566_comment'></div>每命一方镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369566_comment'></div>遂绵历岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369566_comment'></div>就加爵秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369566_comment'></div>以至于没身吊赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369566_comment'></div>自陛下圣泽亭育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369566_comment'></div>天威震曜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369566_comment'></div>吴蜀底定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369566_comment'></div>人神洽和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369566_comment'></div>三四年间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369566_comment'></div>易置节将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369566_comment'></div>出入中外者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369566_comment'></div>凡数十辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369566_comment'></div>执介圭不俟驾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369566_comment'></div>相望于道涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369566_comment'></div>而从史宴安自居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369566_comment'></div>未著勋绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369566_comment'></div>顷来群情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369566_comment'></div>犹望除代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369566_comment'></div>今则因其忧服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369566_comment'></div>可以慎选守臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369566_comment'></div>况卢虔以文学至大官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369566_comment'></div>殁于阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369566_comment'></div>以从史之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369566_comment'></div>自可全儒家丧纪之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369566_comment'></div>宏圣朝孝理之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369566_comment'></div>以从史非贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369566_comment'></div>则连𢖍非人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369566_comment'></div>煽结为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369566_comment'></div>贻朝廷忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369566_comment'></div>恐自此始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369566_comment'></div>且成德事体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369566_comment'></div>与昭义不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369566_comment'></div>众情以为许成德之请则可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369566_comment'></div>许昭义之请则不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369566_comment'></div>以恒冀习俗颇久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369566_comment'></div>倘类相因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369566_comment'></div>含垢推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369566_comment'></div>制之以渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369566_comment'></div>故上党内地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369566_comment'></div>未尝因循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369566_comment'></div>失之毫釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369566_comment'></div>利害相万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369566_comment'></div>或者虑苟未受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369566_comment'></div>则劳王师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369566_comment'></div>诱劫武人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369566_comment'></div>阻拒旬朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369566_comment'></div>臣愚以为凡朝廷计之甚远大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369566_comment'></div>以来至当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369566_comment'></div>倘成命既下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369566_comment'></div>不时率道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369566_comment'></div>邻道戒严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1369566_comment'></div>备于境上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1369566_comment'></div>人各有心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369566_comment'></div>必思自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369566_comment'></div>前秘书省校书郎薛贻谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1369566_comment'></div>比充从史掌书记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1369566_comment'></div>去岁恳求罢免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1369566_comment'></div>归里京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369566_comment'></div>臣比任礼部侍郎日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369566_comment'></div>贻谋进士及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1369566_comment'></div>数与相见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1369566_comment'></div>访其人情泽潞山东事体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1369566_comment'></div>贻谋一二详悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1369566_comment'></div>言其恩信不及于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1369566_comment'></div>若命将以伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1369566_comment'></div>万无所虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1369566_comment'></div>或召贻谋陈奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1369566_comment'></div>亦冀少广聪听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1369566_comment'></div>事更淹缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1369566_comment'></div>转失机宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1369566_comment'></div>臣备位班行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1369566_comment'></div>禀性愚鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1369566_comment'></div>苟有所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1369566_comment'></div>辄披肺肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1369566_comment'></div>得于众多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1369566_comment'></div>事甚明白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1369566_comment'></div>不敢缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1369566_comment'></div>上疏上陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1369566_comment'></div>无任惶惧恳迫陨越之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1369566_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1369566_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_106_1369566_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年4月29日</a>　四月二十九日，迁太常卿，赐紫金鱼袋，散官迁通议大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年7月18日</a>　七月十八日，友人杨凭贬临贺尉，交亲无敢祖送者，独徐晦送至蓝田，权德舆称之于朝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年10月17日</a>　十月十七日，上奏论恒州招讨事宜。作品：恒州招讨事宜状。<div id='poem_1369567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恒州招讨事宜状</a><span class='authorDate'>（809年10月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369567")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369567'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369567'>右。臣伏见诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369567_comment'></div>以王承宗未禀朝命。薛昌朝未赴德州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369567_comment'></div>大兴师徒。以务攻讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369567_comment'></div>中外臣庶。不任愤激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369567_comment'></div>臣伏计数日已来。朝官论用兵害者已多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369567_comment'></div>臣不敢更引烦词。徒惑圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369567_comment'></div>臣今直举管见二事。冒昧上陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369567_comment'></div>一则神策等兵在城中。多是市井屠沽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369567_comment'></div>庇身军籍。未经战阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369567_comment'></div>难以成功。经途既远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369567_comment'></div>所虞非细。或中路溃扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369567_comment'></div>结为萑蒲。未至交锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369567_comment'></div>别有此虑。况恒冀马军素劲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369567_comment'></div>兵数颇多。倘淹时月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369567_comment'></div>则损威重。又西戎淮右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369567_comment'></div>□凶狡多端。或乘间犯边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369567_comment'></div>或干纪出境。禁卫武备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369567_comment'></div>不可顿虚。山东犹疥癣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369567_comment'></div>京师犹心腹也。不可不深以此为念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369567_comment'></div>一则恐须便除成德及德棣两道节度使。则六州之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369567_comment'></div>知有所奉。兵交之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369567_comment'></div>各图自拔。不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369567_comment'></div>则以壤界所接。而尽分其地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369567_comment'></div>如乐寿博野。可以却还瀛州之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369567_comment'></div>使其四邻。各务攻取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369567_comment'></div>则人人自战。而恩归于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369567_comment'></div>不劳师费。则坐剪妖孽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369567_comment'></div>此亦必然之理也。伏惟陛下忧劳之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369567_comment'></div>臣忝备班行。苟有所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369567_comment'></div>不敢缄默。无任惶惧恳悃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369567_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369567_comment'></div>元和四年十月十七日。太常卿权某上奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369567_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1369567_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年3月27日</a>　三月二十七日，上山东行营条件。作品：山东行营事宜状。<div id='poem_1369568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山东行营事宜状</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年3月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369568")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369568'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369568'>一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369568_comment'></div>自去年十月兴师讨罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369568_comment'></div>今已半岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369568_comment'></div>未见成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369568_comment'></div>时渐入夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369568_comment'></div>水潦疾病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369568_comment'></div>众心不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369568_comment'></div>主客相悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369568_comment'></div>若更因循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369568_comment'></div>必虑溃挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369568_comment'></div>窃闻自出师以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369568_comment'></div>已费用五百馀万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369568_comment'></div>物力既屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369568_comment'></div>人心则摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369568_comment'></div>不可不深以此为念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369568_comment'></div>一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369568_comment'></div>山东诸侯未朝觐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369568_comment'></div>各有息男为副大使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369568_comment'></div>其心不相远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369568_comment'></div>孰肯为陛下尽力者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369568_comment'></div>以陛下神武睿图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369568_comment'></div>埽定吴蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369568_comment'></div>凡劝陛下讨王承宗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369568_comment'></div>虽迹似忠荩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369568_comment'></div>其意在于必不成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369568_comment'></div>朝廷惩创。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369568_comment'></div>遂不问山东之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369568_comment'></div>此其计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369568_comment'></div>一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369568_comment'></div>凡举众行师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369568_comment'></div>须因众心喜怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369568_comment'></div>王武俊实有破朱滔之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369568_comment'></div>而地广兵劲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369568_comment'></div>若更淹延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369568_comment'></div>挫损转甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369568_comment'></div>今日中朝公卿大夫之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369568_comment'></div>莫若爱人息众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369568_comment'></div>含垢忍耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369568_comment'></div>沛然下哀痛之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369568_comment'></div>宥其罪辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369568_comment'></div>若更败伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369568_comment'></div>则无所及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369568_comment'></div>一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369568_comment'></div>若以直赦承宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369568_comment'></div>诚人心所便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369568_comment'></div>而师出半岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369568_comment'></div>无功而旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369568_comment'></div>则不若因有制置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369568_comment'></div>使众情有所观听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369568_comment'></div>如卢从史者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369568_comment'></div>诱设陈璀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369568_comment'></div>每事逗遛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369568_comment'></div>贵出草粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369568_comment'></div>贱收缣帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369568_comment'></div>倚寇为援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369568_comment'></div>以邀宠利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369568_comment'></div>其间情伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369568_comment'></div>非止一途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369568_comment'></div>比于承宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369568_comment'></div>其过实甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369568_comment'></div>今若于在近命行营节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369568_comment'></div>令其倍道兼程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369568_comment'></div>度其行至半途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1369568_comment'></div>授以泽潞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1369568_comment'></div>然后别命从史京西已来一镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1369568_comment'></div>既离本处巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1369568_comment'></div>即奸计不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1369568_comment'></div>新授朝命宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1369568_comment'></div>必不虑不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1369568_comment'></div>况闻其贪虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1369568_comment'></div>人心厌苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1369568_comment'></div>有所改更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1369568_comment'></div>必求悦随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369568_comment'></div>若从史除官及除替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369568_comment'></div>并恩宥承宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369568_comment'></div>三道制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1369568_comment'></div>同时涣发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1369568_comment'></div>则众情感浃成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1369568_comment'></div>伏惟试以此为念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369568_comment'></div>一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369568_comment'></div>军储国计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1369568_comment'></div>仰给江淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1369568_comment'></div>江淮旱歉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1369568_comment'></div>人心日急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369568_comment'></div>若连兵不解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369568_comment'></div>则忧患非细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1369568_comment'></div>顷者众情以淮西三州之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1369568_comment'></div>四面劳师费财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1369568_comment'></div>谓必命帅于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1369568_comment'></div>以正王度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1369568_comment'></div>昨者已除吴少阳充留后使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1369568_comment'></div>伏计圣慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1369568_comment'></div>必以爱人为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1369568_comment'></div>含宏覆育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1369568_comment'></div>淮西既犹如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1369568_comment'></div>即承宗理固不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1369568_comment'></div>但在速耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1369568_comment'></div>以前臣自去年四月十五日上奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1369568_comment'></div>以欲变山东之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1369568_comment'></div>先在择昭义帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1369568_comment'></div>恐从史煽结为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1369568_comment'></div>贻朝廷忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1369568_comment'></div>又去年十月十七日上奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1369568_comment'></div>以禁军多市井屠沽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1369568_comment'></div>未经战阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1369568_comment'></div>倘淹时月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1369568_comment'></div>则损威重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1369568_comment'></div>令物情忧骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1369568_comment'></div>思竭肺肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1369568_comment'></div>以陛下圣德圣姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1369568_comment'></div>虚受宏纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1369568_comment'></div>敢以疏贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1369568_comment'></div>上干聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1369568_comment'></div>无任惶惧恳悃迫切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1369568_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1369568_comment'></div>元和五年三月二十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1369568_comment'></div>通议大夫守太常卿臣权德舆奏状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_116_1369568_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年4月</a>　四月，斋荐于太清宫。<br /><a href="javascript: href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年2月</a>　任宰相，二月，权知门下省过官。作品：谢权知门下省过官状。<div id='poem_1369502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢权知门下省过官状</a><span class='authorDate'>（811年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369502")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369502'>右。臣奉恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369502_comment'></div>权知门下省<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1369502", 1369502, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>过官</span>者。伏以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1369502", 1369502, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>过官</span>至重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369502_comment'></div>事在黄枢。阅郡吏之否臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369502_comment'></div>布百职于中外。苟或非当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369502_comment'></div>其伤实多。臣自玷台司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369502_comment'></div>忽及半载。一昨陈乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369502_comment'></div>天眷未回。当忧惕之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369502_comment'></div>而宠荣荐至。摩顶至踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369502_comment'></div>岂酬鸿私。无任感恩荷戴之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369502_comment'></div>谨奉状陈谢以闻。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369502_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1369502_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=812&endYear=812')">812年1月25日</a>　正月二十五日，上请祔庙状。<div id='poem_1369531' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369531?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请祔庙状<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（812年1月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span
