id='poem_title_1369531_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1369531_0'>① 臣亡父先臣秘书省著作郎赠太子少傅某</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369531'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369531'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369531_comment'></div>臣先臣在玄宗朝筮仕河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369531_comment'></div>忠孝名节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369531_comment'></div>冠于当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369531_comment'></div>至德乾元之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369531_comment'></div>历监察御史起居舍人著作郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369531_comment'></div>在代宗朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369531_comment'></div>早违圣代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369531_comment'></div>臣幼丁荼蓼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369531_comment'></div>不及义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369531_comment'></div>过蒙渥恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369531_comment'></div>禄秩崇厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369531_comment'></div>按开元礼文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369531_comment'></div>合立私庙三室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369531_comment'></div>永怀怵惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369531_comment'></div>思展吉蠲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369531_comment'></div>已于通济坊修建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369531_comment'></div>择用二月二十日祔飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369531_comment'></div>臣位忝台司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369531_comment'></div>时逢孝理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369531_comment'></div>事循彝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369531_comment'></div>礼展私诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369531_comment'></div>感戴恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369531_comment'></div>不敢不奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369531_comment'></div>伏听敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1369531_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=812&endYear=812')">812年2月1日</a>　二月一日，上谢追赠先公太子太保表。作品：谢追赠表。<div id='poem_1369527' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369527' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369527?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢追赠表</a><span class='authorDate'>（812年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369527")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369527_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369527'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369527'>臣德舆言。伏奉今日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369527_comment'></div>臣亡父赠太子少傅先臣某追赠太子太保。宠灵所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369527_comment'></div>徽数特加。捧承命书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369527_comment'></div>感奉酸咽。臣某诚惶诚荷顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369527_comment'></div>伏以先臣在天宝末年。筮仕幽朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369527_comment'></div>艰贞特立。忠孝两全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369527_comment'></div>名节冠于古今。风声激乎天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369527_comment'></div>以执宪载笔。逮事肃宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369527_comment'></div>禀命不融。早违昭代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369527_comment'></div>臣龆龀之岁。孤苦零丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369527_comment'></div>遭逢昌运。渐履名级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369527_comment'></div>过叨睿奖。忽至台司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369527_comment'></div>无能受禄。莫与臣比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369527_comment'></div>以先臣之名器未称。馀庆或钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369527_comment'></div>以陛下之宠秩逾涯。此生何幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369527_comment'></div>所建家庙。实稽国章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369527_comment'></div>时及春祠。礼从祔飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369527_comment'></div>岂谓圣慈曲被。孝思是崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369527_comment'></div>当启椟题主之时。有告第漏泉之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369527_comment'></div>感深霜露。礼盛烝尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369527_comment'></div>自叶流根。实荷非常之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369527_comment'></div>摩顶至踵。难酬不次之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369527_comment'></div>幽明交感。山岳非重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369527_comment'></div>无任祗荷陨越之至。谨奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369527_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚荷顿首顿首。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369527_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1369527_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=812&endYear=812')">812年</a>　夏，与李吉甫、李绛对事延英殿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=813&endYear=813')">813年1月7日</a>　正月七日，罢知政事，仍守礼部尚书，时爵已进扶风郡开国公，余如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=813&endYear=813')">813年6月12日</a>　六月二十二日，应诏进旧诗五十首。作品：进诗状。<div id='poem_1369501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进诗状</a><span class='authorDate'>（813年6月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369501")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369501'>右。宰臣奉宣进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369501_comment'></div>令臣进旧诗者。伏惟陛下以圣德文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369501_comment'></div>化成天下。徵诗之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369501_comment'></div>本在枢衡。念旧之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369501_comment'></div>因及簪屦。臣顷尸重任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369501_comment'></div>久旷官常。今列大僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369501_comment'></div>犹叨宠渥。于孔门非赐也言诗之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369501_comment'></div>在汉庭异匡氏说诗之工。徒积繁芜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369501_comment'></div>岂近声律。自承休命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369501_comment'></div>伏用兢惶。待罪之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369501_comment'></div>无补公餗。免退之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369501_comment'></div>犹献雕虫。既乖法言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369501_comment'></div>有黩宸听。震悚怵惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369501_comment'></div>不知所安。谨录前件诗五十首奉进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369501_comment'></div>无任惭惧陨越之至。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369501_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1369501_comment'></div></div></div><br href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=814&endYear=814')">814年10月24日</a>　十月二十四日，复入为太常卿。作品：谢除太常卿表。<div id='poem_1369524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除太常卿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（814年10月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369524")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369524_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369524'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369524'>臣某言。伏奉十月二十四日诏命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369524_comment'></div>除臣太常卿。统和神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369524_comment'></div>典司礼乐。臣实庸菲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369524_comment'></div>谬叨宠荣。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369524_comment'></div>臣以书生凡辈。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1369524", 1369524, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>懦薄</span>无堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369524_comment'></div>生遇昌期。累膺爵秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369524_comment'></div>四掌诰命。五居列曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369524_comment'></div>遂叨礼卿。乃佩相印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369524_comment'></div>竟无微效。上答皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369524_comment'></div>自罢宰司。再履宗伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369524_comment'></div>旋忝保釐之任。属当优寄之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369524_comment'></div>淮甸多虞。周郊接壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369524_comment'></div>上劳圣虑。下辑戎师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369524_comment'></div>臣不敢爱身。不敢避事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369524_comment'></div>频抗手疏。备陈物宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369524_comment'></div>苟披肺肝。莫识忌讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369524_comment'></div>自承诏旨。许募新军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369524_comment'></div>实使懦夫增气。辄思仁者有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369524_comment'></div>缮修器甲。招集骁雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369524_comment'></div>每竭一心。敢有二事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369524_comment'></div>陛下忧臣不逮。全度特深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369524_comment'></div>出于殊私。遽降新命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369524_comment'></div>沐浴皇泽。从容大僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369524_comment'></div>量力无庸。庇身何幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369524_comment'></div>况太常者。伯夷叔孙通之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369524_comment'></div>臣岂其人。五六年间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369524_comment'></div>再居此地。感恩知惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369524_comment'></div>循分难任。即以今月三日进发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369524_comment'></div>瞻望阙庭。踊跃欣忭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369524_comment'></div>谨奉表陈谢以闻。无任感戴喜惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369524_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369524_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1369524_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=815&endYear=815')">815年4月</a>　四月，作文祭婿独孤郁。作品：祭子婿独孤少监文。<div id='poem_1369839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭子婿独孤少监文</a><span class='authorDate'>（815年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369839")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369839'>维元和十年岁次乙未四月壬寅朔六日丁未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369839_comment'></div>外舅太常卿权某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369839_comment'></div>敬以清酌时羞之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369839_comment'></div>致祭于故秘书少监赠绛州刺史独孤郎之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369839_comment'></div>噫嘻大钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369839_comment'></div>生死沄沄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369839_comment'></div>寿夭纷纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369839_comment'></div>古人罕言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369839_comment'></div>岂造化流形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369839_comment'></div>不与其全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369839_comment'></div>或一气滑湣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369839_comment'></div>偶然而然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369839_comment'></div>嗟我子婿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369839_comment'></div>时之令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369839_comment'></div>自诚而明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369839_comment'></div>必协于极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369839_comment'></div>前殿大对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369839_comment'></div>谏垣正色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369839_comment'></div>中台有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369839_comment'></div>东观以直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369839_comment'></div>训辞温雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369839_comment'></div>视草宥密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369839_comment'></div>当时之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369839_comment'></div>必居第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369839_comment'></div>玉立皦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369839_comment'></div>古之渊骞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369839_comment'></div>抗词犯颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369839_comment'></div>勇若诸贲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369839_comment'></div>立不易方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369839_comment'></div>即之也温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369839_comment'></div>道乃前定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369839_comment'></div>实安于仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369839_comment'></div>时惟宪公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369839_comment'></div>先友是敦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369839_comment'></div>既以声子之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369839_comment'></div>复兹戴侯之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369839_comment'></div>欢言戾止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369839_comment'></div>十五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369839_comment'></div>始遇弱冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369839_comment'></div>今才强仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369839_comment'></div>会朝方驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369839_comment'></div>居室同里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369839_comment'></div>爱我以德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369839_comment'></div>忠言在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369839_comment'></div>劳绩尽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369839_comment'></div>疾婴腠理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369839_comment'></div>乞身上言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369839_comment'></div>移亚外史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369839_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1369839", 1369839, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>谢绝</span>人寰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369839_comment'></div>屏居鄠田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369839_comment'></div>冀此宴闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369839_comment'></div>百疴就痊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369839_comment'></div>神理暧昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1369839_comment'></div>万情百身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1369839_comment'></div>孤孀嗷号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1369839_comment'></div>所不忍闻。<div id='poem_sentence_77_1369839_comment'></div>礼逾成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1369839_comment'></div>哀感异类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1369839_comment'></div>昔谓福善。<div id='poem_sentence_82_1369839_comment'></div>惟此可冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1369839_comment'></div>翻翻素旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1369839_comment'></div>东指鼎成。<div -----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a6d45bf95b234d58bfbe8a4d9e8cb976_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a6d45bf95b234d58bfbe8a4d9e8cb976");'><span id='a6d45bf95b234d58bfbe8a4d9e8cb976_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=813&endYear=813')">813年</a>，55岁</div><div id='a6d45bf95b234d58bfbe8a4d9e8cb976' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=813&endYear=813')">813年7月3日</a>　七月三日，制命检校吏部尚书、兼御史大夫、充东都留守，判东都尚书省事。散官迁银青光禄大夫，余如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=813&endYear=813')">813年7月24日</a>　七月二十四日，抵东都，作谢表。作品：东都留守谢上表。<div id='poem_1369525' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369525' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369525?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东都留守谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（813年7月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369525")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369525_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369525'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369525'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369525_comment'></div>伏奉今月三日制命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369525_comment'></div>授臣检校吏部尚书兼御史大夫充东都留守判东都尚书省事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369525_comment'></div>以今月二十四日到东都上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369525_comment'></div>荣渥特加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369525_comment'></div>宠光备至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369525_comment'></div>俯仰印绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369525_comment'></div>惭惧交怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369525_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369525_comment'></div>臣才不出众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369525_comment'></div>禄期代耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369525_comment'></div>因缘文字。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1369525_comment'></div>特沐鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369525_comment'></div>历五曹之贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369525_comment'></div>居九卿之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369525_comment'></div>遂叨大任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369525_comment'></div>忽涉四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369525_comment'></div>智虑孱愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369525_comment'></div>言辞朴讷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369525_comment'></div>徒淹岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369525_comment'></div>莫展涓埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369525_comment'></div>虽竭匪躬之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369525_comment'></div>竟乖陈力之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369525_comment'></div>自免枢务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369525_comment'></div>犹忝春官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369525_comment'></div>才经半岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369525_comment'></div>复授今任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369525_comment'></div>前后所历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369525_comment'></div>皆不因人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369525_comment'></div>无非睿奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369525_comment'></div>以至崇大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369525_comment'></div>况留守所寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369525_comment'></div>东夏式瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369525_comment'></div>在君陈毕公之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369525_comment'></div>兼天官府宪之重。<div id='poem_sentence_38_1369525_comment'></div>式遏匪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369525_comment'></div>整训戎事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369525_comment'></div>用资窃发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369525_comment'></div>必资兼材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369525_comment'></div>岂臣懦薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369525_comment'></div>所宜负荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369525_comment'></div>今兵力至微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369525_comment'></div>武备不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369525_comment'></div>此皆天鉴所察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369525_comment'></div>臣不敢累黩聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1369525_comment'></div>杜其奸情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1369525_comment'></div>亦在早计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1369525_comment'></div>必冀磨砺铅钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1369525_comment'></div>罄竭肝心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1369525_comment'></div>忠以事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1369525_comment'></div>死而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1369525_comment'></div>违离宸眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1369525_comment'></div>感恋阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1369525_comment'></div>以陛下注意之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1369525_comment'></div>誓微臣捐躯之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1369525_comment'></div>无任荷戴屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1369525_comment'></div>谨差押衙试殿中监成党奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1369525_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1369525_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1369525_comment'></div></div></div><br 汉中（兴元）

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=816&endYear=816')">816年10月25日</a>　十月二十五日，以检校吏部尚书兼御史大夫充山南西道节度使，余如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=816&endYear=816')">816年</a>　次临阙驿，逢郑余庆还朝，作诗赠之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年2月</a>　二月，奏请子弟营护迁祔。十五日宪宗优诏批答。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年4月20日</a>　四月二十日，迁先公先太君葬于润州丹徒县，男璩营护。作品：缘迁祔请令子弟营护状。<div id='poem_1369533' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369533' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369533?labeling=true' target='_blank'>缘迁祔请令子弟营护状</a><span class='authorDate'>（817年4月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369533")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369533_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369533'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369533'>山南西道节度观察处置等使银青光禄大夫检校吏部尚书兼兴元尹御史大夫上柱国扶风郡开国公臣权德舆。右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369533_comment'></div>臣亡祖松柏。先在东都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369533_comment'></div>臣幼年流寓江都。夙衅钟罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369533_comment'></div>亡父母于润州安厝。今岁在丁酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369533_comment'></div>是商姓通年。取四月二十日于润州启举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369533_comment'></div>七月十九日于东都迁祔。臣孤单零丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369533_comment'></div>早失严训。宠荣累集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369533_comment'></div>霜露感深。至于岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369533_comment'></div>难遇吉便。常恐忽先犬马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369533_comment'></div>莫展私诚。伏以守土理戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369533_comment'></div>不敢自求营护。欲遣子弟专往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369533_comment'></div>不敢不先事上闻。谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369533_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1369533_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　奏请削检校官兼职并散官勋爵，回充先祖追赠。作品：请追赠先祖故羽林军录事参军状。<div id='poem_1369529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369529?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请追赠先祖故羽林军录事参军状</a><span class='authorDate'>（817年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 id='poem_sentence_1_1369529_comment'></div>文行声实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369529_comment'></div>推重士林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369529_comment'></div>禀命不融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369529_comment'></div>竟沉下位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369529_comment'></div>与当时清名之士席建侯包容苏源明友善特深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369529_comment'></div>唱酬文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369529_comment'></div>各在集录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369529_comment'></div>义方流泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369529_comment'></div>以及先臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369529_comment'></div>忠孝名节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369529_comment'></div>闻于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369529_comment'></div>累蒙追锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369529_comment'></div>备极哀荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369529_comment'></div>逮至微臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369529_comment'></div>实荷祖训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369529_comment'></div>猥以琐劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369529_comment'></div>过叨鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369529_comment'></div>今检校官兼官并至三品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369529_comment'></div>勋官及爵并至二品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369529_comment'></div>玷冒斯甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369529_comment'></div>旷败是忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369529_comment'></div>况臣本官兴元尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369529_comment'></div>足领当道使务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369529_comment'></div>理戎抚俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369529_comment'></div>不假他官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369529_comment'></div>回充亡祖追赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369529_comment'></div>则残生展霜露之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369529_comment'></div>幽壤荷日月之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369529_comment'></div>今先臣改葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369529_comment'></div>輤裧就路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369529_comment'></div>亡祖旧域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369529_comment'></div>松槚是依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369529_comment'></div>倘因此事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369529_comment'></div>特沐恩礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369529_comment'></div>使贻厥之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369529_comment'></div>俯遂良诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369529_comment'></div>罔极之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369529_comment'></div>下申先志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369529_comment'></div>圣朝孝理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369529_comment'></div>横绝古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369529_comment'></div>慺慺肝血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369529_comment'></div>敢此披沥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369529_comment'></div>无任哀恳迫切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369529_comment'></div>谨遣进奏官押衙朝议郎前金牛县主簿张儇奉状陈乞以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369529_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1369529_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年6月</a>　六月，外孙女妹妹、孙奉常相继夭亡，作文哀祭。作品：祭外孙女文；祭孙男法延师文。<div id='poem_1369843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭外孙女文</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369843'>维元和十二年岁次丁酉六月己未朔十二日庚午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369843_comment'></div>外翁婆以清酌庶羞之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369843_comment'></div>致祭于独孤氏孙女妹妹之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369843_comment'></div>吾残生衰苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369843_comment'></div>殃祸相循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369843_comment'></div>四年已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369843_comment'></div>七遘伤悼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369843_comment'></div>今日之痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369843_comment'></div>情又倍常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369843_comment'></div>以前年再丁齐斩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369843_comment'></div>意其孤苦备极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369843_comment'></div>或保安全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369843_comment'></div>神理谓何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369843_comment'></div>又兹夭阏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369843_comment'></div>自婴羸恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369843_comment'></div>虽未痊除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369843_comment'></div>而神用精明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369843_comment'></div>不减平日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369843_comment'></div>昨以晦朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369843_comment'></div>归奉几筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1369843_comment'></div>信宿之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1369843_comment'></div>幽明已隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1369843_comment'></div>奔告惝恍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1369843_comment'></div>如狂如痴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1369843_comment'></div>呼天不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1369843_comment'></div>此痛何极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1369843_comment'></div>况今冬除禫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1369843_comment'></div>来岁初笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1369843_comment'></div>方择良对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1369843_comment'></div>以图先近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1369843_comment'></div>岂吾之薄祜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1369843_comment'></div>有忤神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1369843_comment'></div>复尔之禀命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1369843_comment'></div>不可踰越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1369843_comment'></div>理遣不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1369843_comment'></div>情钟奈何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1369843_comment'></div>吾家壤树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1369843_comment'></div>宛在伊洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1369843_comment'></div>今尔体魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1369843_comment'></div>归祔寿安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1369843_comment'></div>吾多病薾然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1369843_comment'></div>义期可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1369843_comment'></div>生也死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1369843_comment'></div>如环斯循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1369843_comment'></div>倘冥冥有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1369843_comment'></div>冀与尔为泉壤乡党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1369843_comment'></div>沥酒申诀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1369843_comment'></div>呜呼痛深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1369843_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1369843_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1369840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭孙男法延师文</a><span class='authorDate'>（817年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369840")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369840'>维元和十二年岁次丁酉五月庚申朔十三日壬申。翁翁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1369840", 1369840, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>婆婆</span>以乳果之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369840_comment'></div>致祭于九岁孙男法延师之灵。尔之敏悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369840_comment'></div>尔之孝爱。才至龀齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369840_comment'></div>已能知书。倦息犹在于文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369840_comment'></div>嬉游不离于砚席。其姿状有外祖河南之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369840_comment'></div>懿兹夙成。必谓致远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369840_comment'></div>疾疡所遘。医祷无瘳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369840_comment'></div>竟罹夭枉。痛切心骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369840_comment'></div>况自二岁。三哭殇孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369840_comment'></div>逝者日远。存者无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1369840_comment'></div>吾以衰年多病。支体不随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1369840_comment'></div>尔父在京。不见其绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1369840_comment'></div>痛尔槥椟。归遵畏涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1369840_comment'></div>今日哀怀。尤倍常理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1369840_comment'></div>顷者求拔苦海。依归度门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1369840_comment'></div>故于敛袭。率以缁褐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1369840_comment'></div>今之祖奠。靡设膻腥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1369840_comment'></div>苦痛之深。遣割不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1369840_comment'></div>临路长痛。呜呼奈何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1369840_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1369840_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年7月15日</a>　七月十五日，先人迁祔事毕，作告文及祔葬墓志铭等。作品：王妣夫人弘农杨氏祔葬墓志铭。<div id='poem_1369775' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1369775' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1369775?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王妣夫人宏农杨氏祔葬墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（817年7月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15294, "中唐", "权德舆", "poem_title_1369775")'>权德舆</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1369775_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1369775'>王妣夫人姓杨氏。宏农人。祖敏。皇太仆少卿交州都督金乡县公。父晏。湖州武康县令。夫人始笄。归于王考府君。府君名重而禄薄。家肥而身约。仕至左辅尉中兵纪纲掾。所与游者皆天下隽人贤士。夫人无攸遂。劝以义之道备焉。天宝四年。先太保贞孝公既孤。夫人慈仁训育。以文行绍续。繇进士第授临清尉蓟县尉。安禄山之乱也。以大节闻。履险违难。崎岖色养。灭迹人事。以扁舟为家。至德二年。夫人弃孝养于杭州富阳县之行次。时四方兵交。岁大疫。江东尤剧。未克归祔。此焉宁神。先公号咷崩毁。因中风湿痹痛。(一作痼)外除。拜御史著作郎。皆以疾不祗命。大历丁未。德舆丁荼蓼。贞元戊辰。再集艰。馀生未泯。积庆所钟。因缘践履。叨冒崇大。以岁时之不易。事物之多故。久未迁神。心焉若摧。言阴阳者。利在卯酉。元和五年。岁直庚寅。德舆忝太常卿。以明年之吉。襄事既具。其年猥参宰政。礼不克就。乃建宗庙。以严蒸尝。逮今十二岁在丁酉。德舆以检校吏部尚书理戎汉中。拜章上请。协用龟策。启先公先太君寿堂于丹徒。启夫人寿宫于富阳。得七月壬寅祔王考府君兆域于东都伊阙县慈水之阳吉。自杭抵洛。凡二千五百里。水陆安静。诚信无违。天之佑也。惟尊灵幽閟。周一甲子。罪在孱菲。宜当诛殛。而懿范遗训。流光孕休。闺门受祉。施于孙子。霜露怵惕。如惔如酲。又德舆之生也后。不获逮事。逖听令闻。靡详万一。故合姓之纪岁。弃代之享年。皆阙焉。刻兹介石。以永终吉。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1369775_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1369775'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1369775'>惟王母之令德。淑明柔克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1369775_comment'></div>闺门延耀。以引以翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1369775_comment'></div>王父安卑兮。其道未光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1369775_comment'></div>先公大节兮。易名章章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1369775_comment'></div>伊孤孙之蒙騃。不获逮事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1369775_comment'></div>庆灵流泽兮。积累名器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1369775_comment'></div>浙河汤汤。輤车帷裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1369775_comment'></div>伊水之阳。祔于幽堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1369775_comment'></div>万有千岁兮。徽音不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1369775_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1369775_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　元稹上书，呈诗文五十四篇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年8月</a>　任山南西道节度使。八月，因病乞还，诏以崔从代之。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洋县（洋州）
